[BE/AccountingFramework] accounting framework -- framework, including policies, methods, rules, and processes, used to measure, recognize, present, and disclose the information appearing in an entity's financial statements, and, from a legal ownership perspective, that is applied for accounting consolidation determination
[BE/Affiliate] affiliate -- party that is related to a legal entity, directly, or indirectly through one or more intermediaries, and controls, or is controlled by, or is under common control with that entity, typically determined by the degree of ownership
[BE/Affiliation] affiliation -- situation in which a controlled party is affiliated with a controlling party for some period of time
[BE/ArticlesOfIncorporation] articles of incorporation -- contract that establishes a new corporation or, when amended, adjusts the legal basis for the corporation, and outlines basic information about the corporation, including the type of business, and a description of the business' operational characteristics
[BE/Association] association -- not-for-profit organization that is owned by and acts on behalf of its members
[BE/Auditor] auditor -- party qualified and authorized to review and verify the accuracy of financial records and ensure that companies comply with tax laws
[BE/Authorization] Authorization
[BE/AuthorizedIndividual] authorized individual -- role of an individual that has been given the responsibility to act on behalf of another party under some set of guidelines
[BE/AuthorizedParty] AuthorizedParty
[BE/AuthorizingParty] AuthorizingParty
[BE/BeneficialOwner] beneficial owner -- party that enjoys the benefits of ownership (such as receipt of income) of something even though its ownership (title) may be in the name of another party (called a nominee or registered owner)
[BE/BeneficialOwnership] beneficial ownership -- situation linking party that enjoys the benefits of ownership (such as receipt of income) of something even though its ownership (title) may be in the name of another party (called a nominee or registered owner) to the asset that they own
[BE/BenefitCorporation] benefit corporation -- not-for-profit corporation set up under specific state legislation, typically to provide some social benefit, without an obligation to maximize shareholder return
[BE/BoardAgreement] board agreement -- formal, legally binding agreement between members of the Board of Directors of the organization
[BE/BoardCapacity] board capacity -- authority to act in a fiduciary capacity with respect to the organization, including but not limited to determining and executing corporate policy
[BE/BoardCompositionControl] board composition control -- situation in which a voting shareholder, entity owner, or some other party in the case of a not-for-profit organization, appoints and/or nominates someone to the board of directors of an organization for some period of time
[BE/BoardMember] board member -- party that has fiduciary responsibility with respect to the organization, including but not limited to determining and executing corporate policy
[BE/BoardMembership] board membership -- situation relating an individual member of the board of directors to the organization
[BE/BoardOfDirectors] board of directors -- group of people comprising the governing body of an organization that has the authority to set organizational strategy and policies as well as to select and, to some degree manage, leadership
[BE/Branch] branch -- part of a larger organization that might not be co-located with it
[BE/BranchOfGovernment] branch of government -- division of the government of a state, with separate and independent powers and areas of responsibility so that the powers of one branch are not in conflict with the powers associated with the other branches
[BE/BusinessEntity] business entity -- entity that is formed and administered as per commercial law in order to engage in business activities
[BE/BusinessLicense] business license -- license that allows the holder to conduct business or carry out a specific profession within some jurisdiction for some period of time
[BE/Bylaws] bylaws -- written rules for conduct of a corporation, association, partnership or any organization
[BE/CharteredLegalPerson] chartered legal person -- a legal person created by a royal charter or decree
[BE/ChiefExecutiveOfficer] chief executive officer -- top corporate officer responsible for an organization's overall operations and performance  Also a subclass of: BE/ExecutiveBoardMember, BE/PrincipalParty.
[BE/ChiefFinancialOfficer] chief financial officer -- senior-most corporate officer responsible for financial control and planning for an organization or project
[BE/CommonInterestDevelopmentCorporation] common interest development corporation -- not-for-profit corporation set up under specific state legislation as a business entity for homeowners' associations
[BE/CompanyLaw] company law -- legislation under which the formation, registration or incorporation, governance, and dissolution of a firm is administered and controlled
[BE/CompanySecretary] company secretary -- corporate officer appointed by the directors of an organization, responsible for ensuring compliance with legal obligations related to corporate governance
[BE/ConstitutionalOwner] constitutional owner -- entity owner that holds an equity stake in said entity, in the form of shareholders' equity
[BE/ContractualControl] contractual control -- control established through the terms of some contract
[BE/ContractuallyCapableEntity] contractually capable entity -- a unique entity that is legally or financially responsible for the performance of financial transactions, or has the legal right in its jurisdiction to enter independently into legal contracts, regardless of whether it is incorporated or constituted in some other way (e.g. trust, partnership, contractual). This excludes natural persons, but includes governmental organizations and supranationals.
[BE/ControlledAffiliate] controlled affiliate -- controlled party in an affiliation situation  Also a subclass of: BE/Affiliate.
[BE/ControlledParty] controlled party -- person or organization over which some party exercises some form of authority or influence with respect to some situation
[BE/ControllingAffiliate] controlling affiliate -- controlling party in an affiliation situation  Also a subclass of: BE/Affiliate.
[BE/ControllingAlliance] controlling alliance -- group that has formed some alliance to jointly exercise control over some entity
[BE/ControllingEquity] controlling equity -- shareholders's equity that formally confers control in the entity, either by law or as explicitly stated in a corresponding equity instrument
[BE/ControllingNominee] controlling nominee -- party that holds legal title to an asset (e.g., stocks, bonds, or property) on behalf of the beneficial owner
[BE/CooperativeSociety] cooperative society -- organization owned by and operated for the benefit of those using its services
[BE/CorporateBylaws] corporate bylaws -- written rules for conduct of a corporation, adopted by the board of directors
[BE/CorporateOfficer] corporate officer -- high-level management executive of a corporation or other organization, hired by the board of directors or the business owner(s), charged with certain operational responsibilities, and who has the authority to act on behalf of the organization, including the authority to enter into contracts on behalf of the organization  Also a subclass of: BE/Signatory.
[BE/Corporation] corporation -- formal organization that is a legal entity (artificial person) distinct from its owners, created under the jurisdiction of the laws of a state or nation
[BE/CourtAppointedControl] court appointed control -- control conferred by the actions of some court, for example in the context of receivership
[BE/DeFactoControllingInterestParty] de facto controlling interest party -- party that exercises some control over an entity other than via explicit, legal means
[BE/DeJureControllingInterestParty] de jure controlling interest party -- party that has the legal authority to exercise control
[BE/DevolvedGovernment] devolved government -- government and the politicians that that run a subnational territory with powers that may be temporary and reversible, ultimately residing with the central government
[BE/DirectConsolidation] direct consolidation -- direct ownership of an entity recorded as accounting consolidation
[BE/Division] division -- part of an organization, such as a line of business, that may have separate accounting and reporting requirements
[BE/DomesticUltimateParent] domestic ultimate parent -- party that is recognized as the ultimate parent of a given organization within the country or jurisdiction of incorporation or organization
[BE/EntityControllingParty] entity controlling party -- party that has the authority to control some legal entity
[BE/EntityLegalForm] entity legal form -- a classifier for a legal entity that indicates the nature of that entity as defined from a legal or regulatory perspective, in the jurisdiction in which it was established
[BE/EntityLegalFormIdentifier] entity legal form identifier -- code that denotes an entity legal form as defined in ISO 20275
[BE/EntityLegalFormScheme] entity legal form scheme -- scheme that specifies the elements of the codes for entity legal forms, such as those that are sanctioned in a given jurisdiction as defined in ISO 20725
[BE/EntityOwner] entity owner -- owner (person, group of people, or other business entity) that owns, or holds an ownership interest in, a formal business organization
[BE/EntityOwnership] entity ownership -- ownership by some party of an interest in some non-governmental formal organization
[BE/Executive] executive -- person appointed and given the responsibility to manage the affairs of an organization and the authority to make decisions within specified role-specific boundaries
[BE/ExecutiveBoardMember] executive board member -- member of a board of directors that is also an employee of the organization  Also a subclass of: FND/Employee.
[BE/ExecutiveBranch] executive branch -- the branch of government that is authorized and responsible for the daily administration of the government
[BE/ExternalAuditor] external auditor -- independent party qualified and authorized to examine and report on the accuracy of financial records and ensure that companies comply with tax laws
[BE/FamilyOffice] family office -- organization that assumes the day-to-day administration and management of a family's affairs
[BE/FederalGovernment] federal government -- union of states under a central government distinct from the individual governments of the separate states
[BE/FederatedSovereignty] federated sovereignty -- polity characterized by a union of partially self-governing states or regions under a central (federal) government
[BE/ForeignBranchOwnership] foreign branch ownership -- ownership by some party of some formal organization or organizational sub-unit that is a foreign affiliate and legally part of the owning entity
[BE/ForProfitCorporation] for profit corporation -- corporation whose objective is to make money, i.e., to ensure realization of a financial benefit such that the amount of revenue gained from a business activity exceeds the expenses, costs and taxes needed to sustain that activity
[BE/FunctionalBusinessEntity] functional business entity -- functional entity defined in terms of the nature of the commercial activity it conducts
[BE/FunctionalEntity] functional entity -- party defined in terms of a function they or it performs
[BE/GeneralPartner] general partner -- partner and part-owner that is responsible for managing the day to day operations of the partnership and that may be jointly and severally liable for the obligations of the partnership  Also a subclass of: BE/Partner.
[BE/GeneralPartnership] general partnership -- partnership that has at least two general partners that agree to share in all assets, profits, and financial and legal liabilities of the business
[BE/GlobalUltimateParent] global ultimate parent -- party that is recognized as the ultimate parent of a given organization world-wide
[BE/Government] government -- system by which a state or community is controlled
[BE/GovernmentAgency] government agency -- permanent or semi-permanent organization, often an appointed commission, in the machinery of government that is responsible for the oversight and administration of specific functions
[BE/GovernmentAppointee] government appointee -- individual designated by government decree to lead, or participate in some capacity in a government body  Also a subclass of: BE/Executive.
[BE/GovernmentBody] government body -- formal organization that is an agency, instrumentality, or other body of a supranational, national, federal, state, or local government, including certain multijurisdictional agencies and departments that carry out the business of government
[BE/GovernmentDepartment] government department -- specialized organization responsible for a sector of government public administration
[BE/GovernmentMinister] government minister -- government official that is an executive, who is either appointed or elected to a high office in the government  Also a subclass of: BE/Executive.
[BE/GovernmentOfficial] government official -- person elected or appointed to administer some aspect of a government
[BE/IncorporationGuarantee] incorporation guarantee -- guarantee that is part of the financial basis by which some legal entity is incorporated
[BE/InfluenceBasedDeFactoControl] influence-based de facto control -- informal control that involves influence over some party
[BE/InfluenceBasedDeFactoControllingParty] influence-based de facto controlling party -- party that holds influence-based control over some other party
[BE/Instrumentality] instrumentality -- organization that serves a public purpose and is closely tied to a government, but is not a government agency
[BE/InstrumentOfIncorporation] instrument of incorporation -- memorandum and articles of association by which some legal entity is established
[BE/InternalAuditor] internal auditor -- employee who is qualified and authorized to review and verify the accuracy of financial records and evaluate internal controls and compliance  Also a subclass of: FND/Employee.
[BE/InvestmentBasedDeFactoControl] investment-based de facto control -- control that arises through some investment in some entity, other than via the holding of constitutional equity (shares etc.) in that entity
[BE/InvestmentBasedDeFactoControllingInterestParty] investment-based de facto controlling interest party -- party that holds investment-based control over some other party  Also a subclass of: BE/Investor.
[BE/InvestmentEquity] investment equity -- equity that represents an ownership interest in some entity, but may or may not take the form of shareholders's equity
[BE/Investor] investor -- party that owns some stake in some organization by way of investment  Also a subclass of: FND/ContractParty.
[BE/InvestorContract] investor contract -- Contract setting out the terms under which some investor invests in the entity and setting out the rights which are conferred on that investor.
[BE/IrrevocableTrust] irrevocable trust -- trust that cannot be modified, amended or terminated except under certain legal circumstances and typically not without the permission of the grantor's named beneficiary or beneficiaries
[BE/JointControllingParty] joint controlling party -- party that collectively has the authority to control the affairs of some business organization
[BE/JointStockCompany] joint stock company -- for-profit, unincorporated business that has some characteristics of a corporation and some features of a partnership, with ownership interests represented by shares of stock
[BE/JointVenture] joint venture -- legal entity that is formed between parties that pool their resources for the purpose of accomplishing a specific task but otherwise retain their distinct identities
[BE/JointVenturePartner] joint venture partner -- party that shares capital, technology, human resources, risks, and benefits of an entity under shared control
[BE/Judiciary] judiciary -- branch of government that comprises the system of courts that interprets and applies the law in the name of the supranational, national, federal, or regional government, depending on its jurisdiction
[BE/LegalEntityIdentifier] legal entity identifier -- an organization identifier that uniquely identifies a legal person as defined in ISO 17442
[BE/LegalEntityIdentifierScheme] legal entity identifier scheme -- a scheme that specifies the elements of an unambiguous legal entity identifier (LEI) scheme to identify the legal entities relevant to any financial transaction
[BE/LegallyCompetentNaturalPerson] legally competent natural person -- person who is considered competent, under the circumstances, to enter into a contract, conduct business, or participate in other activities that generally require the mental ability to understand problems and make decisions on his or her own behalf
[BE/LegallyDelegatedAuthority] LegallyDelegatedAuthority
[BE/Legislature] legislature -- the law-making body of a political unit, usually a national government, that has power to enact, amend, and repeal public policy
[BE/LEIRegisteredEntity] LEI registered entity -- a legal person that has registered for and is identified by a legal entity identifier
[BE/LimitedLiabilityCompany] limited liability company -- private limited company that combines the pass through taxation of a sole proprietorship or partnership with the limited liability of a corporation
[BE/LimitedLiabilityCompanyMember] limited liability company member -- owner of an interest in a limited liability company  Also a subclass of: BE/EntityControllingParty, BE/EntityOwner.
[BE/LimitedLiabilityCompanyTaxedAsACorporation] limited liability company taxed as a corporation -- limited liability company that has elected to have corporate tax status
[BE/LimitedLiabilityLimitedPartnership] limited liability limited partnership -- limited partnership that consists of one or more general partners who are liable for the obligations of the entity as well as one or more protected limited liability partners
[BE/LimitedLiabilityPartnership] limited liability partnership -- partnership that has general partners but provides its individual partners some level of protection against personal liability for certain partnership liabilities
[BE/LimitedPartner] limited partner -- partner whose liabilities are limited to the extent of their investment or guarantees and that has no involvement in the day to day operations of the partnership
[BE/LimitedPartnership] limited partnership -- partnership that has at least one general partner and at least one limited partner
[BE/LivingTrust] living trust -- trust created during an individual's lifetime where a designated person, the trustee, is given responsibility for managing that individual's assets for the benefit of the eventual beneficiary
[BE/MajorityControllingParty] majority controlling party -- controlling party that possesses, either directly or indirectly, the power to direct or cause the direction of the management and policies of a legal person, whether through the ownership of a majority of voting securities, by contract, or otherwise
[BE/ManagerManagedLimitedLiabilityCompany] manager-managed limited liability company -- limited liability company in which the members appoint one or more managers to handle the daily operations and administrative responsibilities of the organization
[BE/ManagingMember] managing member -- owner of an interest in a limited liability company who also runs the day-to-day business operations  Also a subclass of: BE/LimitedLiabilityCompanyMember.
[BE/MarketDataProvider] market data provider -- publisher of data relevant to financial markets
[BE/Merchant] merchant -- party engaged in the purchase and sales of goods produced by others for profit
[BE/MerchantCategoryCode] merchant category code -- code used internationally to classify a merchant
[BE/MerchantCategoryCodeScheme] merchant category code scheme -- scheme defining a set of codes for classifying merchant services
[BE/MerchantIdentifier] merchant identifier -- unique identifier for a merchant that is used, for example, for transaction interchange purposes
[BE/MunicipalEntity] municipal entity -- polity that typically represents a city, township, or other administrative subdivision having corporate status and powers of self-government or jurisdiction
[BE/MunicipalGovernment] municipal government -- regional government of a city, township, or other administrative subdivision
[BE/NationalGovernment] national government -- government and the politicians that that run a country as a whole (as opposed to local government)
[BE/NonExecutiveBoardMember] non-executive board member -- member of the board of directors of an organization that has no executive responsibilities towards the running of that organization
[BE/NonGovernmentalOrganization] non-governmental organization -- not-for-profit organization that functions independently of government
[BE/NotForProfitCorporation] not-for-profit corporation -- corporation approved by its jurisdictional oversight and tax authorities as operating for educational, charitable, social, religious, civic or humanitarian purposes  Also a subclass of: BE/NotForProfitOrganization.
[BE/NotForProfitObjective] not for profit objective -- objective that reflects the charitable, educational, religious, humanitarian, public services, or other not for profit goals of an organization
[BE/NotForProfitOrganization] not for profit organization -- organization that uses its surplus revenues to further achieve its purpose rather than distributing its surplus income to the organization's owners (directors, investors, and equivalents) as profit / dividends
[BE/OrganizationCoveringAgreement] organization covering agreement -- contract between the principals in a formal organization that specifies the relationship between the principals, and between the principals and the entity
[BE/Partner] partner -- co-owner, member, and agent of a partnership whose participation level, including proportional liabilities and share in the profit / loss of the business is specified in a partnership agreement
[BE/Partnership] partnership -- association of two or more legal persons to carry on as co-owners a business for profit
[BE/PartnershipAgreement] partnership agreement -- contract between partners in a partnership that establishes the terms and conditions of the relationship between the partners
[BE/Polity] polity -- legal person that is a supranational entity, crown, state, or subordinate civil authority, such as a province, prefecture, county, municipality, city, or district representing the people of that entity
[BE/PowerOfAttorney] power of attorney -- legal authorization given by one party (the principal) to another (the agent or attorney-in-fact) to perform certain acts on the principal's behalf
[BE/PrincipalParty] principal party -- controlling party that is responsible for the management of daily business operations of an organization
[BE/PrivateCompanyWithLimitedLiability] private company with limited liability -- hybrid business entity having characteristics of both a corporation and a partnership or sole proprietorship (depending on how many owners there are)
[BE/PrivateLimitedCompany] private limited company -- private limited company whose shareholders' liability is limited to the capital they originally invested
[BE/PrivatelyHeldCompany] privately held company -- corporation whose issued shares are all held by a family or a small group of investors and, therefore, cannot be bought by the public
[BE/ProfitObjective] profit objective -- objective that reflects pursuit of a financial benefit that may be realized when the amount of revenue gained from a business activity exceeds the expenses, costs and taxes needed to sustain that activity
[BE/Publication] publication -- document offered for general distribution and usually produced in multiple copies
[BE/PubliclyHeldCompany] publicly held company -- corporation whose shares are traded and held publicly
[BE/PublicPurpose] public purpose -- objective that reflects values generally thought to be shared by and that is intended to benefit the populace as a whole
[BE/Publisher] publisher -- role of person(s) or organization(s) responsible for the printing or distribution of an item, whether in digital or print (physical) form
[BE/PurchaseLot] purchase lot -- financial asset that is a block of securities or other financial assets bought in one transaction on a given date at a specific price
[BE/Receiver] receiver -- party appointed by some court for the purposes of winding up the affairs of some entity which is no longer solvent
[BE/RegionalGovernment] regional government -- administrative body for a geographic area, such as a county, smaller town, or other similar community
[BE/RegionalSovereignty] regional sovereignty -- legal person that corresponds to an administrative division, administrative unit, administrative entity or country subdivision (or, sometimes, geopolitical division or subnational entity), that has the capacity to incur debt, issue contracts, and enter into relations with other similar entities
[BE/RegistrationIdentifier] registration identifier -- identifier that is officially allocated to an organization at the time of registration, typically in a jurisdiction in which said organization is organized or registered and used in that jurisdiction to identify the organization
[BE/RegistrationIdentifierScheme] registration identifier scheme -- scheme that defines the registration identifier per the issuing registration authority
[BE/RelationshipPeriodQualifier] relationship period qualifier -- a classifier that qualifies something about the reporting period specified, such as that the date period reflects an accounting or document filing period
[BE/RelationshipQualifier] relationship qualifier -- a classifier that qualifies something about the relationship between consolidated entities during the reporting period, such as the accounting framework used
[BE/RelationshipRecord] relationship record -- a record describing relationships between legal entities
[BE/RelationshipStatus] relationship status -- a classifier that specifies the status of the relationship between consolidated entities during the reporting period (active or inactive)
[BE/ReligiousCorporation] religious corporation -- not-for-profit corporation whose objective is specific to some fundamental set of beliefs and practices generally agreed upon by a number of people, and that is incorporated under the law
[BE/ReligiousObjective] religious objective -- not-for-profit objective that reflects the religious goals of an organization
[BE/RevocableTrust] revocable trust -- trust in which legal ownership of the trust property is transferred to the trustee, but the trustor retains full power to revoke, modify or amend the trust
[BE/Shareholder] shareholder -- party that owns shares in and has rights and responsibilities with respect to some asset, provided in exchange for investment  Also a subclass of: FND/Counterparty.
[BE/Shareholding] shareholding -- ownership interest in the equity of a company, represented by shares that confer financial rights and governance privileges
[BE/Signatory] signatory -- responsible party authorized to sign agreements on behalf of themselves, another person, or an organization
[BE/SignificantShareholder] significant shareholder -- party that owns a significant voting stake in an organization that is less than 50 percent but greater than some threshold
[BE/SoleControllingParty] sole controlling party -- party that has sole control over and directs the affairs of some legal entity
[BE/SoleProprietor] sole proprietor -- party that owns a business, has the rights to all profits from that business and is considered a single entity (unincorporated) together with that business for tax and liability purposes
[BE/SoleProprietorship] sole proprietorship -- unincorporated business owned by a single person
[BE/SovereignState] sovereign state -- non-physical juridical entity that is represented by one centralized government that has sovereignty over a geographic area
[BE/SpecialPurposeVehicle] fonds commun de placement -- legal entity created to fulfill narrow, specific, and frequently temporary objectives
[BE/StatutoryBody] statutory body -- legal entity established by a government to consider evidence and make judgements in some field of activity
[BE/StockCorporation] stock corporation -- corporation that has shareholders, each of whom receives a portion of the ownership of the corporation through shares of stock
[BE/Subsidiary] subsidiary -- legal entity that is entirely or majority owned and controlled by another legal entity
[BE/SupranationalEntity] supranational entity -- governmental or non-governmental entity that is established by international law or treaty or incorporated at an international level
[BE/Syndicate] syndicate -- temporary, self-organizing group of people, companies, corporations or entities organized as an alliance whose purpose is to transact some specific business, or to pursue or promote a shared interest
[BE/SyndicateMember] syndicate member -- role of an individual or organization that is a member of an alliance set up to pool resources and share risk with respect to a large transaction
[BE/TaxLot] tax lot -- financial asset that is a block of securities or other financial assets with a distinct cost basis for tax reporting purposes
[BE/TestamentaryTrust] testamentary trust -- trust established in accordance with the instructions contained in a last will and testament
[BE/TotalControllingInterestParty] total controlling interest party -- voting shareholder that owns 100 percent of the voting shares in some legal entity  Also a subclass of: BE/SignificantShareholder.
[BE/TotalOwner] total owner -- party that has 100 percent ownership some legal entity
[BE/TribalArea] tribal area -- designation for geographic region administered by a group of indigenous people rather than by a sovereign state or regional governmental entity
[BE/TribalEntity] tribal entity -- legal entity that represents fundamental unit of sovereign tribal (indigenous) government
[BE/TribalGovernment] tribal government -- government representing a group of indigenous people that has legal authority to govern those people, including authority to legislate the existence of tribal entities
[BE/Trust] trust -- fiduciary relationship and legal entity in which one party, known as a trustor, gives another party, the trustee, the right to hold title to and manage assets for the benefit of a third party, the beneficiary
[BE/TrustAgreement] trust agreement -- formal agreement that establishes a trust, whereby the trustor(s) gives the trustee(s) the responsibility to hold and manage assets for the beneficiary(ies)
[BE/TrustBeneficiary] trust beneficiary -- party for whose interest (benefit) an annuity, assignment (such as a letter of credit), contract, insurance policy, judgment, promise, trust, will, etc., is made
[BE/Trustee] trustee -- party that holds and manages assets for the benefit of another
[BE/TrustFundManager] trust fund manager -- party empowered to act on behalf of the trustee to manage the assets of the trust
[BE/Trustor] trustor -- party that establishes a trust and places property under the protection and management of one or more trustees for the benefit of at least one beneficiary
[BE/UltimateConsolidation] ultimate ownership -- highest-level (top, end) ancestral ownership, evidenced by accounting consolidation, by some party of some other legal entity
[BE/ValueAddedTaxIdentificationNumber] value-added tax identification number -- tax identifier that identifies a taxable person (business) or non-taxable legal entity for a consumption tax that is assessed incrementally, levied on the price of a product or service at each stage of production, distribution, and sale to the end consumer
[BE/VariableInterestEntity] variable interest entity -- legal entity whose shareholders are entitled to a percentage of a named company's profits via a private contract
[BE/VotingShareholder] voting shareholder -- shareholder whose shares confer the right to vote in corporate elections, including the right to elect directors at annual or special meetings, and to express their views to corporate management and directors on significant issues that may affect the value of those shares  Also a subclass of: BE/Shareholder.
[DER/AccountChangeNotificationObligation] account change notification obligation -- obligation to notify a counterparty of any changes in account details
[DER/AgriculturalResource] agricultural resource -- negotiable commodity that is obtained via some agricultural process, including forestry, fishing, livestock, grain, dairy, corn, cocoa, soybeans, sugar, coffee
[DER/AllotmentRight] allotment right -- privileges allotted to existing security holders, entitling them to receive new securities free of charge  Also a subclass of: FBC/Entitlement.
[DER/AllotmentRightFormula] allotment right formula -- rule applied to calculate the number of securities for an allotment right, typically based on the number of these instruments that the holder holds
[DER/AsianOption] Asian option -- option whose exercise terms involve a payoff determined by the average underlying price (either the strike price or the settlement price) of the underlying asset over a predetermined period
[DER/AsianOptionClassifier] Asian option classifier -- financial instrument classifier that classifies Asian options based on whether they are rate-based or price based
[DER/AssetBackedCreditDefaultSwap] asset-backed credit default swap -- credit default swap whose underlying reference obligation is an asset-backed security rather than corporate credit
[DER/AveragingStrategy] averaging strategy -- method used for calculating the average rate or price of an Asian option
[DER/BarrierCapitalProtectionCertificate] barrier capital protection certificate -- capital-protected product whose protection is defined as a percentage of the nominal price (e.g. 100 percent), with minimum redemption at expiry equivalent to the capital protection  Also a subclass of: DER/ParticipationCertificate.
[DER/BarrierDiscountCertificate] barrier discount certificate -- participation certificate that enables the investor to acquire the underlying asset at a lower price in return for a limited payout, and for which the maximum redemption amount (Cap) is paid out if the barrier is never breached  Also a subclass of: SEC/StructuredFinanceWithoutPrincipalProtection.
[DER/BarrierInstrumentBasedMiniFutureCertificate] barrier instrument-based mini-future certificate -- mini-future certificate that immediately expires if the barrier instrument trading price level is breached during product lifetime
[DER/BarrierOption] barrier option -- option whose final exercise depends upon the path taken by the price of an underlying instrument, i.e., whose payoff depends on whether or not the underlying asset has reached or exceeded a predetermined price
[DER/BarrierReverseConvertibleCertificate] barrier reverse convertible certificate -- participation certificate whose payout is conditional: should the barrier never be breached, the nominal price plus coupon is paid at redemption; if the barrier is breached the product changes into a reverse convertible  Also a subclass of: SEC/StructuredFinanceWithoutPrincipalProtection.
[DER/BarrierUnderlyingMiniFutureCertificate] barrier underlying mini-future certificate -- mini-future certificate that immediately expires if the barrier underlying level is breached during product lifetime
[DER/BaseMetal] base metal -- common metal that tarnishes, oxidizes, or corrodes relatively quickly when exposed to air or moisture, that is widely used in commercial and industrial applications, such as construction and manufacturing
[DER/BasisSwap] basis swap -- swap in which payment streams are referenced to different bases
[DER/BasketCertificate] basket certificate -- certificate whose underlying asset represents a fraction of a basket of securities that corresponds to the subscription ratio
[DER/BasketCreditDefaultSwap] basket credit default swap -- credit default swap that references a bespoke, synthetic portfolio of underlying assets whose components have been agreed to for a specific OTC derivative by the parties to the transaction
[DER/BasketFuture] basket future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is a basket of securities and/or indices
[DER/BasketOfCommodities] basket of commodities -- custom basket whose constituents consist of one or more negotiable commodities
[DER/BasketOfCreditDefaultSwaps] basket of credit default swaps -- basket of reference obligations are credit default swap instruments  Also a subclass of: FND/DatedStructuredCollection.
[DER/BasketOfDebtInstruments] basket of debt instruments -- basket of securities whose constituents are debt instruments
[DER/BasketOption] basket option -- option whose underlying asset is a group, or basket, of commodities, securities, indices, or currencies
[DER/BasketWarrant] basket warrant -- warrant that permits the holder to acquire a package or group of assets at a specified price during a specified period
[DER/BondFuture] bond future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one bond
[DER/BondOption] bond option -- option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to buy or sell (depending on whether it is a call or a put) a bond at a certain price on or before a specified date
[DER/BondPurchaseRight] bond purchase right -- purchase right that gives a prospective acquiree's bondholders the right to buy bonds of the firm or bonds of anyone who acquires the firm at a deep discount to their fair market value
[DER/BondSubscriptionRight] bond subscription right -- subscription right entitling existing bond holders to subscribe to new securities at a price normally lower than the prevailing market price
[DER/BonusCertificate] bonus certificate -- certificate whose minimum redemption is equal to the nominal value provided the barrier has not been breached, with a greater risk in relation to multiple underlying asset(s) (worst-of), allowing for a higher bonus level or lower barrier, and with a reduced risk compared to a direct investment into the underlying asset(s)
[DER/Bullion] bullion -- physical precious metal that is officially recognized as being at least 99.5 percent pure
[DER/Butterfly] butterfly -- strategy that combines bull and bear spreads with a fixed risk and capped profit
[DER/CalculationAgent] CalculationAgent
[DER/CallOption] call option -- option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to buy the assets specified at a fixed price or formula, on or before a specified date
[DER/CallPutWarrant] call put warrant -- warrant that either does not specify call or put features, or that explicitly includes both a call and put feature  Also a subclass of: DER/PutWarrant.
[DER/CallWarrant] call warrant -- warrant giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to acquire specific underlying assets during a specified period at a specified price
[DER/CapitalizedLeaseObligationDebtBasket] capitalized lease obligation debt basket -- basket of debt instruments whose constituents are contracts entitling a renter the temporary use of an asset and, in accounting terms, has asset ownership characteristics
[DER/CapitalProtectedProduct] capital-protected product -- structured product that participates in the performance of a financial asset, such as a stock, fund or index, while protecting the investor's capital
[DER/CapitalProtectionCertificateWithCoupons] capital protection certificate with coupons -- capital-protected product whose protection is defined as a percentage of the nominal price (e.g. 100 percent), with minimum redemption at expiry equivalent to the capital protection  Also a subclass of: DER/ParticipationCertificate.
[DER/CapitalProtectionCertificateWithParticipation] capital protection certificate with participation -- capital-protected product whose protection is defined as a percentage of the nominal amount (e.g. 100 percent), with minimum redemption at expiry equivalent to the capital protection  Also a subclass of: DER/ParticipationCertificate.
[DER/CapitalProtectionConvertibleCertificate] capital protection convertible certificate -- capital-protected product whose protection is defined as a percentage of the nominal price (e.g. 100 percent), with minimum redemption at expiry equivalent to the capital protection  Also a subclass of: DER/ParticipationCertificate.
[DER/CappedOption] capped option -- option with an established profit cap or cap price
[DER/CashflowExpression] cashflow expression -- expression that specifies a calculation of a cash flow as a component of a cashflow formula
[DER/CashflowFormula] cashflow formula -- formula for determining cashflows for a derivative instrument
[DER/CashflowTerms] cashflow terms -- terms setting out a cashflow structure of payments committed to by one party to a contract  Also a subclass of: FBC/DebtTerms.
[DER/CashSettlementMethod] cash settlement method -- strategy for calculating or otherwise establishing a reference final price for the contract
[DER/ChooserOption] chooser option -- exotic option that allows its holder (buyer) to exercise the right to buy (call) or sell (put) specified assets at a fixed price whereby the buyer does not have to decide whether the contract will be a put or a call until an agreed future date, prior to expiration
[DER/CliquetOption] cliquet option -- exotic option that is a series of at-the-money (ATM) options, either puts or calls, where each successive option becomes active when the previous one expires
[DER/Collar] collar -- option trading strategy that involves buying a downside put and selling an upside call that is implemented to protect against large losses, but which also limits large upside gains
[DER/CombinedInstrumentsPurchaseRight] combined instruments purchase right -- purchase right that gives a prospective acquiree's holders of multiple securities the right to buy securities of the firm or securities of anyone who acquires the firm at a deep discount to their fair market value
[DER/CombinedInstrumentsSubscriptionRight] combined instruments subscription right -- subscription right entitling existing holders of multiple securities to subscribe to new securities at a price normally lower than the prevailing market price
[DER/CommodityBasketConstituent] commodity basket constituent -- component of a custom commodity basket whose relative importance with respect to other basket constituents is known
[DER/CommodityDerivative] commodity derivative -- derivative instrument whose primary underlying item is a physical commodity, or the price, or related index, or any other aspect related to a physical commodity  Also a subclass of: FBC/DerivativeInstrument.
[DER/CommodityDerivativeUnderlier] commodity derivative underlier -- underlier of a commodity derivative, including, but not limited to, the negotiable commodity itself
[DER/CommodityForward] commodity forward -- forward contract in which a buyer and seller agree upon delivery of a specified quality and quantity of goods at a specified future date  Also a subclass of: DER/Forward.
[DER/CommodityFuture] commodity future -- futures contract to buy or sell a predetermined amount of a commodity at a specific price on a specific date in the future  Also a subclass of: FBC/Future.
[DER/CommodityIndex] commodity index -- investment vehicle that tracks a basket of commodities to measure their price and investment return performance
[DER/CommodityOption] commodity option -- option where the option buyer has the right to buy or sell specified commodities or commodity related index at a fixed price or formula, on or before a specified date  Also a subclass of: DER/VanillaOption.
[DER/CommodityReturnLeg] commodity return leg -- leg of a commodity return swap in which the return is based on a physical commodity, or the price, or behavior of the price, or any other aspect related to a physical commodity
[DER/CommoditySpotContract] commodity spot contract -- contract that involves physical delivery of the commodity asset at settlement  Also a subclass of: FBC/SpotContract.
[DER/CommoditySwap] commodity swap -- commodity derivative that includes, without limitation, any swap for which the primary underlying notional item is a physical commodity, or the price, or behavior of the price, or the level of a commodity index, or other aspect related to a physical commodity  Also a subclass of: DER/ReturnSwap.
[DER/CommodityWarrant] commodity warrant -- warrant that permits the holder to acquire a specified amount of a commodity during a specified period at a specified price  Also a subclass of: DER/Warrant.
[DER/CommodoreOption] commodore option -- exotic option consisting of a number of digital barrier options that pay a coupon if a pre-determined level of the underlying or basket of underlyings is reached
[DER/CommonConvertibleSharePurchaseRight] common convertible share purchase right -- purchase right that gives a prospective acquiree's common, convertible shareholders the right to buy common, convertible shares of the firm or common, convertible shares of anyone who acquires the firm at a deep discount to their fair market value
[DER/CommonConvertibleShareSubscriptionRight] common convertible share subscription right -- subscription right entitling existing common convertible shareholders to subscribe to new securities at a price normally lower than the prevailing market price
[DER/CommonSharePurchaseRight] common share purchase right -- purchase right that gives a prospective acquiree's common shareholders the right to buy common shares of the firm or common shares of anyone who acquires the firm at a deep discount to their fair market value
[DER/CommonShareSubscriptionRight] common share subscription right -- subscription right entitling existing common shareholders to subscribe to new securities at a price normally lower than the prevailing market price
[DER/CompanyWarrant] CompanyWarrant
[DER/CompoundOption] compound option -- exotic option for which the underlying asset is another option
[DER/CondorSpread] condor spread -- non-directional options strategy that limits both gains and losses while seeking to profit from either low or high volatility
[DER/ConstantLeverageCertificate] constant leverage certificate -- entitlement that combines the structure of an open-end certificate with a leverage option with no fixed term, making leverage available without a term restriction, without a knock-out barrier dependency  Also a subclass of: FBC/Entitlement, FBC/Option.
[DER/ContingentCreditDefaultSwap] contingent credit default swap -- credit default swap in which an additional triggering event is required
[DER/ContractForDifference] contract for difference -- cash-settled derivative where the parties agree to exchange on the maturity of the contract the difference between the current value of the underlying asset and the initial value of that asset when the contract is initiated
[DER/ContributionDebtBasket] contribution debt basket -- basket of debt instruments that allows a company to incur an amount of indebtedness that is equal to (or in top tier sponsor transactions in the U.S., up to two times) the amount of equity contributed to the group
[DER/CorrelationLeg] correlation leg -- floating leg of a correlation swap that pays an amount based on the observed average correlation of the prices of a collection of underlying products
[DER/CorrelationSwap] correlation swap -- over-the-counter statistical derivative that allows one to hedge risks associated with the observed average correlation of a collection of underlying products
[DER/CoveredCall] covered call -- call option in which the seller (investor) owns an equivalent amount of the underlying security
[DER/CoveredWarrant] covered warrant -- warrant that gives the holder the right, but not the obligation, to buy (call warrant) or to sell (put warrant) an underlying asset at a specified price (the strike or exercise price) by a predetermined date, issued without an accompanying security by a third party that holds as many securities as would be required if all the warrants are exercised
[DER/CreditDefaultSwap] credit default swap -- bilateral contract in which one party (protection seller) agrees to provide payment to the other party (protection buyer) should a credit event occur against the underlying, which could be a specified debt (the reference obligation), a specific debt issuer (reference entity), a basket of reference entities and/or reference obligations, or a credit index (reference index)  Also a subclass of: DER/Swap.
[DER/CreditDefaultSwapIndex] credit default swap index -- index whose underlying reference obligations are credit default swap instruments
[DER/CreditDerivative] credit derivative -- derivative instrument that is a privately held, negotiable bilateral contract traded over-the-counter (OTC) between two parties in a creditor/debtor relationship, enabling the creditor to effectively transfer some or all of the risk of a debtor defaulting to a third party
[DER/CreditEventNotice] credit event notice -- irrevocable written or verbal notice that states that a triggering event has occurred
[DER/CreditFacilityDebtBasket] credit facility debt basket -- basket of securities whose constituents are credit agreements that allow the borrower to periodically take out money over an extended period of time rather than reapplying for a loan every time they need funds
[DER/CreditProtectionTerms] credit protection terms -- legal terms that define triggering events and associated conditions related to settlement
[DER/CrossCurrencyInterestRateSwap] cross-currency interest rate swap -- interest rate swap in which the two streams of interest payments are in different currencies
[DER/CurrencyDerivative] currency derivative -- agreement to deliver and settle a given amount of money in one currency, in exchange for a given amount in another currency at an agreed rate of exchange  Also a subclass of: FBC/DerivativeInstrument.
[DER/CurrencyForward] currency forward -- agreement to deliver and settle a given amount of money in one currency, in exchange for a given amount in another currency, at an agreed date in the future and at an agreed rate of exchange  Also a subclass of: DER/Forward.
[DER/CurrencyForwardOutright] currency forward outright -- forward contract in a foreign exchange market that locks in the price at which an entity must buy or sell a currency on a future date
[DER/CurrencyFuture] currency future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is an agreement to exchange a specified amount of one currency for another at some point in the future based on pricing stated in the contract  Also a subclass of: DER/FinancialFuture.
[DER/CurrencyOption] currency option -- option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to buy or sell currency at a specified exchange rate during a specified period of time  Also a subclass of: DER/VanillaOption.
[DER/CurrencySpotContract] currency spot contract -- foreign-exchange contract for immediate delivery  Also a subclass of: FBC/SpotContract.
[DER/CurrencySpotForwardSwap] currency spot forward swap -- foreign exchange agreement between two parties involving an exchange of two currencies at agreed fixed rates: a) on the spot settlement date and b) a reverse exchange on a later specified date
[DER/CurrencySwap] currency swap -- foreign exchange agreement between two parties to exchange a given amount of one currency for another currency for spot delivery or for forward delivery at an agreed rate after a specified period of time  Also a subclass of: DER/Swap.
[DER/CurrencyVolatilityOption] currency volatility option -- currency option whose underlying asset is based on the volatility of a foreign exchange rate
[DER/CurrencyWarrant] currency warrant -- warrant that permits the holder to acquire a specified amount in a certain currency at a specified exchange rate during a specified period  Also a subclass of: DER/Warrant.
[DER/DebtInstrumentDerivative] debt instrument derivative -- security-based derivative whose underlier is a debt observable
[DER/DebtInstrumentFuture] debt instrument future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one debt instrument  Also a subclass of: DER/DebtInstrumentDerivative.
[DER/DebtWarrant] debt warrant -- warrant that permits the holder to acquire a specified amount of a debt instrument or related debt observable a specified period at a specified price  Also a subclass of: DER/DebtInstrumentDerivative.
[DER/DeliverableObligation] deliverable asset -- asset that must be delivered as a part of the process of settling a credit default swap
[DER/DeliverableObligationBuyer] deliverable obligation buyer -- contract party that is obliged to purchase a deliverable obligation (asset) if a triggering event occurs, depending on the event and the contract  Also a subclass of: FND/Buyer.
[DER/DeliverableObligationSeller] deliverable obligation seller -- contract party that is obliged to sell a deliverable obligation (asset) if a triggering event occurs, depending on the event and the contract  Also a subclass of: FND/Seller.
[DER/DerivativeCreditSupportAgreement] derivative credit support agreement -- addendum to the master agreement that governs the exchange of collateral between parties in derivatives transactions
[DER/DerivativeMasterAgreement] derivative master agreement -- master agreement covering derivatives transactions to be carried out between the parties to this contract  Also a subclass of: FND/MasterAgreement.
[DER/DerivativesClearingOrganization] derivatives clearing organization -- clearing house that enables parties to substitute the credit of the DCO for the credit of the parties
[DER/DerivativeSettlementTerms] derivative settlement terms -- settlement terms specifying additional details with respect to what is to be delivered when, to whom, under what conditions at the time of settlement  Also a subclass of: FBC/SettlementTerms.
[DER/DerivativeTerms] derivative terms -- contractual terms specific to derivative contracts, including terms related to payments and delivery between parties
[DER/DigitalOption] digital option -- exotic option that has a pre-determined payout if the option is in-the-money and the payoff condition is satisfied
[DER/DiscountCertificate] discount certificate -- participation certificate that enables the investor to acquire the underlying asset at a lower price in return for a limited payout, and for which the underlying asset(s) and/or a cash amount is redeemed should the underlying asset close below the strike on expiry, for which, in return, the potential profit is capped  Also a subclass of: SEC/StructuredFinanceWithoutPrincipalProtection.
[DER/DispersionLeg] dispersion leg -- floating leg of a dispersion swap that pays an amount based on the realized dispersion of the price changes of the underlying product
[DER/DispersionSwap] dispersion swap -- statistical derivative used to hedge on the magnitude of a price movement of an underlying asset
[DER/DispersionSwapIndexConstituentsLeg] dispersion swap index constituents leg -- dispersion leg whose underlier is a defined set of constituents of a given equity index
[DER/DispersionSwapIndexLeg] dispersion swap index leg -- dispersion leg whose underlier is an equity index
[DER/DividendAdjustmentPeriod] dividend adjustment period -- date period used to calculate the difference, if any between an anticipated dividend and the actual dividend distributed in that period
[DER/DividendFuture] dividend future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one stock dividend  Also a subclass of: DER/EquityDerivative.
[DER/DividendLeg] dividend leg -- floating leg of a dividend swap
[DER/DividendSwap] dividend swap -- equity swap that has at least one leg whose underlier is a dividend stream
[DER/DoubleBarrierOption] double barrier option -- barrier option applied to currencies or over the counter stocks that works as a binary, or digital option in that it pays out only under defined circumstances, or it is worthless, at expiration
[DER/EconomicRateBasedDerivative] economic rate-based derivative -- rate-based derivative whose underlier is some economic indicator
[DER/EconomicRateBasedDerivativeInstrument] EconomicRateBasedDerivativeInstrument
[DER/EconomicRateObservable] EconomicRateObservable
[DER/EnergyResource] energy resource -- negotiable commodity that is an energy-related product, or a derivative of an energy-related product, including electricity, renewable energy, or any power/energy delivered through a utility network of provider; diesel fuel, fuel oil, gas oil, gasoline, heating oil, jet fuel, kerosene, natural gas, oil (Brent, Tapis, Dubai, WTI)
[DER/EnergyTransmissionRights] energy transmission rights -- rights to the transmission of power across an electricity distribution network
[DER/EnvironmentalResource] environmental resource -- negotiable commodity including offset credits
[DER/EquityCorrelationSwap] equity correlation swap -- correlation swap that allows one to hedge risks associated with the observed average correlation of a collection of underlying equity products  Also a subclass of: DER/EquitySwap.
[DER/EquityDerivative] equity derivative -- security-based derivative whose underlier is based on equities (e.g. shares, basket of equities or index) or their cashflow(s)
[DER/EquityForward] equity forward -- forward contract to buy or sell the underlying equity stock, equity index, basket of equity stock, equity futures contract, or equity option at a specified future date at the price specified at the outset of the contract
[DER/EquityFuture] equity future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one equity security, specifically a publicly issued and traded share  Also a subclass of: DER/EquityDerivative.
[DER/EquityOption] equity option -- option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to buy (via a call option) or sell (via a put option) the underlying equity assets specified at a pre-determined price (i.e., the strike price, fixed or calculated), on or before a specified date (the expiration date)  Also a subclass of: DER/EquityDerivative.
[DER/EquityPriceReturnSwap] equity price return swap -- return swap whose return leg underlier is based on equities  Also a subclass of: DER/EquitySwap.
[DER/EquityReturnLeg] equity return leg -- return leg whose income is based on equities
[DER/EquitySwap] equity swap -- swap whose payments are linked to the change in value of underlying equities (e.g. shares, basket of equities or index) or their cashflow(s)  Also a subclass of: DER/EquityDerivative.
[DER/EquityTotalReturnSwap] equity total return swap -- total return swap whose return leg underlier is based on equities  Also a subclass of: DER/EquitySwap.
[DER/EquityVarianceSwap] equity variance swap -- dispersion swap in which the parties agree to exchange payments based on the difference between (i) the realized variance of the price changes of a specified equity underlier over a stated observation period and (ii) a fixed amount of variance that is agreed when the contract is executed  Also a subclass of: DER/EquitySwap.
[DER/EquityVolatilitySwap] equity volatility swap -- dispersion swap that is a forward contract on the variability of movements in the price of its underlying equities  Also a subclass of: DER/EquitySwap.
[DER/EquityWarrant] equity warrant -- warrant that permits the holder to acquire a specified amount of an equity instrument during a specified period at a specified price  Also a subclass of: DER/TraditionalWarrant, DER/EquityDerivative.
[DER/EscrowAgent] escrow agent -- third party that holds an asset or funds before they are formally transferred from one party to another party, per the terms of a contract, within some specified time period and/or when a triggering event occurs  Also a subclass of: FND/ContractThirdParty.
[DER/ExcessReturnSwap] excess return swap -- return swap in which the change in the level of the index will be equal to the returns generated primarily by the changes in price of each of the contracts that comprise the index
[DER/ExchangeTradedWarrant] exchange-traded warrant -- warrant that is listed on a securities exchange  Also a subclass of: SEC/ListedSecurity.
[DER/ExoticOption] exotic option -- option that has a non-standard payout structure or other feature  Also a subclass of: FBC/Option.
[DER/ExoticWarrant] exotic warrant -- warrant that gives the holder the right (but not the obligation) to buy (or sometimes sell) an underlying asset under non-standard or complex conditions, often involving additional features not found in a plain vanilla (standard) warrant
[DER/ExpressCertificate] express certificate -- participation certificate whose payout is conditional: should the underlying trade above the strike on the observation date, an early redemption consisting of nominal price plus an additional coupon amount is paid  Also a subclass of: SEC/StructuredFinanceWithoutPrincipalProtection.
[DER/ExtractionResource] extraction resource -- negotiable commodity that is a mineral resource obtained via withdrawal from the natural environment
[DER/ExtrinsicValue] extrinsic value -- measure of the difference between the market price of an option, called the premium, and its intrinsic value
[DER/Fence] fence -- option trading strategy that uses options to limit the range of possible returns on a financial instrument
[DER/FertilizerResource] fertilizer resource -- negotiable commodity that includes ammonia, diammonium phosphate (DAP), potash, sulphur, urea, urea and ammonium nitrate (UAN)
[DER/FinancialFuture] financial future -- futures contract based on underlying assets excluding commodities
[DER/FixedFixedInterestRateSwap] fixed fixed interest rate swap -- interest rate swap in which both parties pay a fixed interest rate that they could not otherwise obtain outside of a swap arrangement
[DER/FixedFloatCrossCurrencyInterestRateSwap] fixed float cross-currency interest rate swap -- interest rate swap in which fixed interest payments on the notional are exchanged for floating interest payments and the two streams of interest payments are in different currencies  Also a subclass of: DER/FixedFloatInterestRateSwap.
[DER/FixedFloatInterestRateSwap] fixed float interest rate swap -- interest rate swap in which fixed interest payments on the notional are exchanged for floating interest payments
[DER/FixedFloatSingleCurrencyInterestRateSwap] fixed float single currency interest rate swap -- interest rate swap in which fixed interest payments on the notional are exchanged for floating interest payments and where both payment streams are expressed in terms of the same currency
[DER/FixedIncomeOption] fixed income option -- option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to buy (via a call option) or sell (via a put option) the underlying fixed income assets specified at a pre-determined price (i.e., the strike price, fixed or calculated), on or before a specified date (the expiration date)  Also a subclass of: DER/DebtInstrumentDerivative.
[DER/FixedInterestRateLeg] fixed interest rate leg -- fixed leg that specifies fixed interest amounts and terms for the payment of that interest  Also a subclass of: DER/InterestRateSwapLeg.
[DER/FixedLeg] fixed leg -- swap leg whose paying party is obligated to make payments from time to time over the term of a swap calculated by reference to a fixed annual rate or consisting of at least one payment of a fixed amount
[DER/FixedLookbackStrikeExpression] fixed lookback strike expression -- cashflow expression specifying the arguments required to calculate the fixed price at which the lookback option is to be exercised
[DER/FixedPaymentLeg] fixed payment leg -- swap leg that specifies contractual terms associated with a schedule of payments for any swap calculated by reference to a fixed annual rate
[DER/FloatFloatCrossCurrencyInterestRateSwap] float float cross-currency interest rate swap -- interest rate swap that exchanges cashflows based on two different interest rates in different currencies
[DER/FloatFloatInterestRateSwap] float float interest rate swap -- interest rate swap that exchanges cashflows based on two different floating interest rates  Also a subclass of: DER/InterestRateSwap.
[DER/FloatFloatSingleCurrencyInterestRateSwap] float float single currency interest rate swap -- interest rate swap that exchanges cashflows based on two different floating interest rates in the same currency
[DER/FloatingInterestRateLeg] floating interest rate leg -- floating leg in which variable interest is paid on some notional amount, linked to some underlying interest reference rate  Also a subclass of: DER/InterestRateSwapLeg.
[DER/FloatingLeg] floating leg -- swap leg whose paying party is obligated to make payments from time to time over the term of a swap calculated by reference to some variable rate, calculated based on the change in value of some underlying asset, or consisting of at least one payment of some floating amount
[DER/FloatingLookbackStrikeExpression] floating lookback strike expression -- cashflow expression specifying the arguments required to calculate the best projected price at which the lookback option may be exercised
[DER/ForeignExchangeMasterAgreement] foreign exchange master agreement -- product-specific master agreement intended to reflect best market practice and to provide a standard agreement for participants in the foreign exchange markets
[DER/ForeignExchangeRateObservable] ForeignExchangeRateObservable
[DER/ForeignExchangeSettlementNettingProvision] foreign exchange settlement netting provision -- settlement netting provision that is specific to foreign exchange contracts
[DER/Forward] forward -- derivative instrument that is privately negotiated between parties to buy the underlier at a specified future date at the price specified in the contract  Also a subclass of: FBC/DerivativeInstrument.
[DER/ForwardContractAdjustmentMethod] forward contract adjustment method -- method by which adjustments will be made to the contract should one or more of a number of extraordinary events occur
[DER/ForwardRateAgreement] ForwardRateAgreement
[DER/ForwardStartOption] forward start option -- exotic option that is fully specified with respect to a set expiry date, underlying asset and other parameters, purchased and paid for on initiation, but that becomes active at a set activation date with a strike price determined at the time of activation
[DER/FreightResource] freight resource -- negotiable commodity that is a freight index route
[DER/FutureOnFuture] future on future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one (other) futures contract
[DER/FutureOnOption] future on option -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one option contract
[DER/FutureOnSwap] future on swap -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one swap contract
[DER/GasCommodity] gas commodity -- extraction resource that is natural gas  Also a subclass of: DER/ExtractionResource.
[DER/GeneralDebtBasket] general debt basket -- basket of debt instruments that provides additional capacity for potential funding and does not require the proceeds to be used for any particular purpose
[DER/GeneratedResource] generated resource -- negotiable commodity obtained via some generation process, including electricity, renewable energy, or any power/energy delivered through a utility network or provider
[DER/GrainCommodity] grain commodity -- agricultural resource that is a small, hard seed, of a food plant, especially of a cereal plant, such as wheat, corn, rye, oats, rice, and millet
[DER/IncrementalFacilityDebtBasket] incremental facility debt basket -- basket of credit facilities whose constituents are extensible, allowing companies to borrow an additional term loan or revolving credit facility (or increase the commitments applicable thereto) under the same credit agreement subject to certain parameters
[DER/IndexCertificate] index certificate -- certificate whose underlying asset is an index
[DER/IndexCreditDefaultSwap] index credit default swap -- credit default swap that references a family of standardized credit derivative indices, where the underlying reference entities are a defined basket of credit from a particular geographic region (e.g. Asia, North America, Europe), and/or credit rating level (e.g. emerging markets, high yield, investment grade)
[DER/IndexFuture] index future -- futures contract whose underlying asset is at least one reference index or economic indicator
[DER/IndexReturnSwap] index return swap -- return swap in which payments are based on a fee paid to the seller of the swap and on a floating reference price based on changes in the level of an index from an initial level to a level observed on some valuation date(s)
[DER/IndexTrancheCreditDefaultSwap] index tranche credit default swap -- credit default swap that references a synthetic collateralized debt obligation (CDO) based on a credit index where each tranche references a different segment of the loss distribution of the underlying index
[DER/IndexWarrant] index warrant -- warrant that permits the holder to acquire a specified amount based on the performance of an index during a specified period at a specified price
[DER/IndustrialResource] industrial resource -- negotiable commodity that is obtained via some industrial process, including construction and manufacturing
[DER/InflationLeg] inflation leg -- floating rate leg of an inflation swap linked to an inflation index, such as the Consumer Price Index (CPI)
[DER/InflationSwap] inflation swap -- rate swap in which one party pays an amount calculated using an inflation rate index, and the other party pays an amount calculated using another inflation rate index, or a fixed or floating interest rate  Also a subclass of: DER/RatesSwap.
[DER/InterestRateCapOption] interest rate cap option -- interest rate derivative in which the buyer receives payments at the end of each period in which the interest rate exceeds the agreed strike price
[DER/InterestRateDerivative] interest rate derivative -- rate-based derivative whose underlier is an interest rate
[DER/InterestRateDerivativeInstrument] InterestRateDerivativeInstrument
[DER/InterestRateFloorOption] interest rate floor option -- interest rate derivative in which the buyer receives payments at the end of each period in which the interest rate is below the agreed strike price
[DER/InterestRateFuture] interest rate future -- futures contract with an interest-bearing instrument as the underlying asset
[DER/InterestRateObservable] InterestRateObservable
[DER/InterestRateOption] interest rate option -- option that giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to receive a cash payment if market interest rate of a reference rate is higher or lower, depending on the option, than the strike rate of the option  Also a subclass of: DER/VanillaOption.
[DER/InterestRateSwap] interest rate swap -- swap in which the reference (underlier) for at least one leg is an interest rate  Also a subclass of: DER/RatesSwap.
[DER/InterestRateSwapLeg] interest rate swap leg -- swap leg that has an interest rate payment stream, including both a parametric and cashflow representation for the stream of payments
[DER/IntrinsicValue] intrinsic value -- measure of what an asset is worth, i.e. with respect to its current price
[DER/IntroducingBroker] introducing broker -- broker that solicits or accepts orders for derivatives that are traded on or subject to the rules of an exchange  Also a subclass of: FBC/Broker.
[DER/IronButterfly] iron butterfly -- butterfly strategy that consists of two call options and two put options, three strike prices and the same expiration date
[DER/IronCondor] iron condor -- condor strategy consisting of two puts (one long and one short) and two calls (one long and one short), and four strike prices, all with the same expiration date
[DER/KnockInOption] knock-in option -- barrier option that is not triggered until a certain price threshold is met
[DER/KnockOutOption] knock-out option -- barrier option with a built-in mechanism to expire as worthless if a specified price level in the underlying asset is reached
[DER/LeveragedProduct] leveraged product -- structured product that provides a further enhanced yield (over and above that of a yield-enhancement product), often without any limit to the upside participation, and frequently with a stop-loss in order to limit potential capital losses
[DER/LoanCreditDefaultSwap] loan credit default swap -- credit default swap whose underlying reference obligation is limited strictly to syndicated secured loans, rather than any type of corporate debt
[DER/LocalLinesOfCreditDebtBasket] local lines of credit debt basket -- basket of debt instruments that may be relevant for companies with international operations, often permitting debt to be incurred by a non-guarantor restricted subsidiary
[DER/LongMiniFutureCertificate] long mini-future certificate -- mini-future certificate that typically entitles the holder to acquire specific underlying assets during a specified period at a specified price
[DER/LongTermEquityAnticipationSecurity] long-term equity anticipation security -- equity option that allows the holder to buy or sell shares of stock with expiration dates that are longer than one year, and typically up to three years from issue
[DER/LookbackOption] lookback option -- exotic option that minimizes the uncertainties related to the timing of market entry, providing the holder the advantage of knowing history when determining when to exercise their option
[DER/LookbackStrikeTerms] lookback strike terms -- terms specifying the value of the underlying asset based on analysis during a specific period, typically ending in the maturity of the option, whereby the payoff is determined by comparing the strike price with the value of the selected price
[DER/LowExercisePriceOption] low exercise price option -- exotic option that is a European-style call option with an exercise price of one cent that mimics a futures contract  Also a subclass of: DER/ExoticOption.
[DER/MajorSwapParticipant] major swap participant -- financial service provider that maintains a substantial position in swaps for any of the major swap categories
[DER/MasterAgreementEarlyTerminationRight] master agreement early termination right -- contractual right of a party to the master agreement to terminate the agreement early
[DER/MeatCommodity] meat commodity -- agricultural resource derived from the flesh of an animal (especially a mammal), such as pork bellies
[DER/Metal] metal -- material that, when freshly prepared, polished, or fractured, shows a lustrous appearance, and conducts electricity and heat relatively well
[DER/MiniFutureCertificate] mini-future certificate -- entitlement that combines the structure of an open-end certificate with a leverage option with no fixed term, making leverage available without a term restriction, and whose payoff depends on whether or not the underlying asset has reached or exceeded a predetermined price  Also a subclass of: DER/SecurityBasedDerivative, FBC/Entitlement.
[DER/MoneyMarketFuture] money market future -- futures contract with a money market instrument as the underlying asset
[DER/Moneyness] moneyness -- classifier for a derivative relating its strike price to the price of its underlying asset
[DER/MountainRangeOption] mountain range option -- exotic option based on multiple underlying securities
[DER/MultiNameCreditDefaultSwap] multi-name credit default swap -- credit default swap that references more than one obligation or borrower
[DER/NakedWarrant] naked warrant -- warrant that gives the holder the right, but not the obligation, to buy (call warrant) or to sell (put warrant) an underlying asset at a specified price (the strike or exercise price) by a predetermined date, issued without an accompanying security by a third party that does not hold as many securities as would be required if all the warrants are exercised
[DER/Non-GuarantorDebtBasket] non-guarantor debt basket -- basket of debt instruments that include a provision allowing certain subsidiaries within a corporate group, which are not part of the loan guarantee, to incur a specified amount of indebtedness
[DER/NotifyingParty] notifying party -- party responsible for issuing one or more formal notices indicating that an event that is relevant to a given contract has taken place
[DER/NotionalStepAmount] notional step amount -- the amount of money that is subtracted from the notional on each step date
[DER/NotionalStepChangeEvent] notional step change event -- event in which a step change in the notional amount for a given swap leg occurs  Also a subclass of: SEC/StepEvent.
[DER/NotionalStepPeriodLength] notional step period length -- recurrence interval indicating the frequency with which step changes occur, which is a multiple of the calculation period in the calculation schedule
[DER/NotionalStepSchedule] notional step schedule -- schedule of changes in the notional amount on which interest is paid, comprising the regular sequence of step events  Also a subclass of: SEC/StepSchedule.
[DER/ObservableValue] observable value -- specification for the value for something discernible and for which evidence can be obtained
[DER/ObservedBestValue] observed best value -- observed value of the underlying asset as of some date during the lookback period that is considered the best value from the perspective of the option holder during the lookback period (depending on whether the option is a call or put)
[DER/OilCommodity] oil commodity -- generated resource that is a viscous liquid derived from petroleum, including for use as fuel, or as a lubricant, and the manufacture of many types of paints, plastics, and other materials
[DER/OilGrade] oil grade -- measure of the viscosity of oil during operation
[DER/OptionHolder] option holder -- party that owns an option
[DER/OptionIssuer] option issuer -- issuer granting the rights defined in the option in exchange for some consideration
[DER/OptionOnFuture] option on future -- option that gives the holder the right, but not the obligation, to buy or sell a specific futures contract at a specified price on or before the option's expiration date
[DER/OptionPremium] option premium -- current market price of an option contract
[DER/OptionPremiumFormula] option premium formula -- expression used to calculate the premium based either on the price per option or percentage of the notional amount
[DER/OptionTradingStrategy] option trading strategy -- trading tactic involving more than one option type, strike price, or expiration date on the same underlying asset
[DER/OutperformanceBonusCertificate] outperformance bonus certificate -- certificate that allows disproportionate participation (outperformance) in positive performance above the strike, in which the minimum redemption is equal to the nominal value provided the barrier has not been breached, with greater risk multiple underlying asset(s) (worst-of) allow for a higher bonus level or lower barrier, and reduced risk compared to a direct investment into the underlying asset(s)  Also a subclass of: DER/OutperformanceCertificate.
