[DER/OutperformanceCertificate] outperformance certificate -- certificate that allows disproportionate participation (outperformance) in positive performance above the strike, reflecting underlying price moves 1:1 (adjusted by the conversion ratio and any related fees), and whose risk is comparable to direct investment in the underlying asset(s)
[DER/OvernightIndexSwap] overnight index swap -- swap in which the periodic payments for one leg are based on an overnight interest rate index multiplied by the same notional amount upon which payments for the other leg of the swap are based
[DER/OvernightRateIndexLeg] overnight rate index leg -- floating leg in which periodic payments are based on an overnight interest rate index multiplied by the same notional amount on which the payments for the other leg of the swap are based
[DER/OverTheCounterDerivativeInstrument] over-the-counter derivative instrument -- derivative instrument that is not listed on an organized exchange  Also a subclass of: FBC/DerivativeInstrument.
[DER/OverTheCounterInstrument] over-the-counter instrument -- financial instrument and bilateral contract that is not listed on an organized exchange
[DER/PaperResource] paper resource -- negotiable commodity that is a paper product, including containerboard, newsprint, pulp, recovered paper
[DER/ParametricCashflowTerms] parametric cashflow terms -- terms for a set of cashflows defined according to a mathematical formula
[DER/ParticipationCertificate] participation certificate -- participation product that provides the possibility to participate in the gains or losses in the price of an asset, subject to counterparty risk  Also a subclass of: SEC/StructuredFinanceInstrument.
[DER/ParticipationInstrument] participation instrument -- structured product that provides the possibility to participate in the performance of an asset or basket of assets  Also a subclass of: DER/SecurityBasedDerivative.
[DER/PayingParty] paying party -- party responsible for making payments in a transaction specified in a contract  Also a subclass of: FND/Payer, FND/Buyer.
[DER/PerformanceBasedVariableLeg] performance-based variable leg -- floating leg of a swap that depends on some statistical measure of the performance of the underlier
[DER/PerpetualWarrant] perpetual warrant -- warrant without an expiration date, giving the holder the right, but not the obligation, to buy (call warrant) or to sell (put warrant) an underlying asset at a certain strike price
[DER/PlainVanillaInterestRateSwap] plain vanilla interest rate swap -- fixed-float single currency interest rate swap in which interest payments are netted, the notional principal does not change, and there are no embedded options
[DER/PolypropyleneResource] polypropylene resource -- negotiable commodity including plastics
[DER/PreferredConvertibleSharePurchaseRight] preferred convertible share purchase right -- purchase right that gives a prospective acquiree's preferred, convertible shareholders the right to buy preferred, convertible shares of the firm or preferred, convertible shares of anyone who acquires the firm at a deep discount to their fair market value
[DER/PreferredConvertibleShareSubscriptionRight] preferred convertible share subscription right -- subscription right entitling existing preferred, convertible shareholders to subscribe to new securities at a price normally lower than the prevailing market price
[DER/PreferredSharePurchaseRight] preferred share purchase right -- purchase right that gives a prospective acquiree's preferred shareholders the right to buy preferred shares of the firm or preferred shares of anyone who acquires the firm at a deep discount to their fair market value
[DER/PreferredShareSubscriptionRight] preferred share subscription right -- subscription right entitling existing preferred shareholders to subscribe to new securities at a price normally lower than the prevailing market price
[DER/PrivateWarrant] private warrant -- warrant that is not tradable  Also a subclass of: FBC/NonNegotiableSecurity.
[DER/ProjectedValueAtMaturity] projected value at maturity -- expected value of the underlying asset at maturity calculated as of some date during the lookback period
[DER/ProtectiveCollar] protective collar -- collar that consists of a covered call and protective put
[DER/ProtectivePut] protective put -- put option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to sell the assets specified at with a strike price equal or close to the current price of the underlying asset, on or before a specified date
[DER/PublicWarrant] public warrant -- warrant that may be traded over the counter (OTC) or through an exchange  Also a subclass of: FBC/NegotiableSecurity.
[DER/PurchaseRight] purchase right -- anti-takeover device that gives a prospective acquiree's shareholders the right to buy shares of the firm or shares of anyone who acquires the firm at a deep discount to their fair market value
[DER/PutOption] put option -- option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to sell the assets specified at a fixed price or formula, on or before a specified date
[DER/PutWarrant] put warrant -- warrant giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to sell the assets specified (i.e., acquire cash in exchange for the underlying assets, such as stock) back to the issuer at a fixed price or formula, on or before a specified date
[DER/QualifyingDividendPeriod] qualifying dividend period -- date period over which the sum of all qualifying dividends paid by the relevant issuers as identified in the swap terms is calculated
[DER/RainbowOption] rainbow option -- exotic option linked to the performances of two or more underlying assets
[DER/RateBasedDerivative] rate-based derivative -- derivative instrument where the holder has the right but may not have the obligation, depending on the nature of the instrument, to enter into the underlying contract, or pay or receive payment related to the underlying financial rate (or rate contract) on a specified future date based on a specified future rate and term
[DER/RateBasedDerivativeInstrument] RateBasedDerivativeInstrument
[DER/RateBasedLeg] rate-based leg -- swap leg of a rate-based swap based on a floating interest, floating inflation or fixed interest rate
[DER/RateBasedObservable] RateBasedObservable
[DER/RatesSwap] rates swap -- swap in two counterparties each agree to pay the other cash flows on defined dates during an agreed period, based on a specified notional amount and a floating interest, floating inflation or fixed interest rate
[DER/RatioDebtBasket] ratio debt basket -- basket of debt instruments whose constituents are specified based on a leverage ratio based on total debt rather than only secured debt
[DER/RealizedVariableLeg] realized variable leg -- performance-based leg wherein the payment is netted at maturity rather than periodically
[DER/ReceivingParty] receiving counterparty -- party that receives payments in a transaction specified in a contract  Also a subclass of: FND/Payee, FND/Seller.
[DER/ReturnLeg] return leg -- leg of a swap in which the income generated by some underlier is paid
[DER/ReturnSwap] return swap -- swap in which one leg, the return leg, is based on income generated from some underlier
[DER/ReverseConvertibleCertificate] reverse convertible certificate -- participation certificate whose payout is conditional: should the underlying asset close below the strike on expiry, the underlying asset(s) and/ or a cash amount is redeemed; should the underlying asset close above the strike at expiry, the nominal amount plus the coupon is paid at redemption  Also a subclass of: SEC/StructuredFinanceWithoutPrincipalProtection.
[DER/RiskReversal] risk reversal -- option trading strategy that consists of being short (selling) an out of the money put and being long (i.e., buying) an out of the money call, both with the same maturity
[DER/SecurityBasedDerivative] security-based derivative -- derivative instrument whose underlier is based on a security, including collections of securities and indices based on securities
[DER/ServiceResource] service resource -- negotiable commodity involving services such as transportation, communications, and trade
[DER/SettlementAuction] settlement auction -- independently administered synthetic auction process on a set of defined deliverable obligations that sets the reference final price that can be used to facilitate cash settlement of all covered transactions following a credit event
[DER/ShortMiniFutureCertificate] short mini-future certificate -- mini-future certificate that entitles the holder to acquire cash in exchange for specific underlying assets
[DER/SimpleReturnLeg] simple return leg -- return leg based strictly on the income generated by the underlying asset, excluding appreciation, decrease in value, capital gains, and fees on any increase in value
[DER/SingleCurrencyInterestRateSwap] single currency interest rate swap -- interest rate swap in which the two streams of interest payments are in the same currency
[DER/SingleNameCreditDefaultSwap] single name credit default swap -- credit default swap whose underlying risk is a single reference obligation, or a single reference entity, such as a corporation or a sovereign borrower
[DER/SpecialDividendLegTerms] special dividend leg terms -- terms that are invoked if special dividend and memorial dividends are applicable
[DER/StandardizedFuturesListingTerms] standardized futures listing terms -- contract terms established by a derivatives exchange that apply to any listing of a futures contract on that exchange.  Also a subclass of: FBC/StandardizedTerms.
[DER/StandardizedFuturesTerms] standardized futures terms -- contract terms established by a derivatives exchange that apply to any futures contract traded on that exchange  Also a subclass of: FBC/StandardizedTerms.
[DER/StandardizedOptionsTerms] standardized options terms -- standardized contract terms established by a securities or options exchange or by an options clearing entity
[DER/StatisticalSwap] statistical swap -- swap that depends on some statistical measure of the performance of the underlier
[DER/Straddle] straddle -- neutral option trading strategy that involves simultaneously buying both a put option and a call option for the underlying security with the same strike price and the same expiration date
[DER/Strangle] strangle -- option trading strategy in which the investor holds a position in both a call and a put option with different strike prices, but with the same expiration date and underlying asset
[DER/StrikeLeg] strike leg -- swap leg that specifies a fixed amount, 'the strike', quoted at the time of execution
[DER/StrikePrice] strike price -- price at which a lot of the underlying asset may be bought or sold when the contract is exercised
[DER/StripStrategy] strip strategy -- option trading strategy that involves a sequential set of options with periodic reset dates, such that each period between resets behaves like an individual option
[DER/StructuredProduct] structured product -- security whose cash flow characteristics depend upon one or more indices or that have embedded forwards or options or securities where an investor's investment return and the issuer's payment obligations are contingent on, or highly sensitive to, changes in the value of underlying assets, indices, interest rates or cash flows
[DER/StructuredWarrant] structured warrant -- warrant that is listed on an exchange, offering investors a way to participate in the price performance of an underlying asset without buying it directly
[DER/SubscriptionRight] subscription right -- privileges allotted to existing security holders, entitling them to subscribe to new securities at a price normally lower than the prevailing market price
[DER/Swap] swap -- derivative instrument whereby counterparties agree to exchange periodic streams of cash flows or liabilities from two different financial instruments with each other
[DER/SwapConfirmation] swap confirmation -- formal confirmation that codifies the terms and conditions specific to a lifecycle event with respect to the overall transaction between the parties  Also a subclass of: FND/TransactionConfirmation.
[DER/SwapDataRepository] swap data repository -- financial service provider that provides a central facility for swap data reporting and recordkeeping
[DER/SwapDealer] swap dealer -- non-depository institution such as one that deals in swaps, makes a market in swaps, regularly enters into swaps with counterparties as an ordinary course of business for its own account, and engages in any activity causing the person to be commonly known in the trade as a dealer/market maker in swaps  Also a subclass of: FBC/Dealer.
[DER/SwapLeg] swap leg -- terms defining and the commitment to fulfill cashflow requirements (e.g., interest payments, coupon payments, etc.) for a component of a swap  Also a subclass of: DER/SwapTerms.
[DER/SwapLegEvent] swap leg event -- swap lifecycle event, such as a payment or rate reset event, that applies to one leg of a swap
[DER/SwapLifecycleEvent] swap lifecycle event -- event that occurs during the lifecycle of a swap, where the overall set of events includes those specific to the issuer, front office, middle office, and/or back office processes
[DER/SwapLifecycleEventIdentifier] swap lifecycle event identifier -- identifier that uniquely identifies a specific event in the lifecycle of a swap
[DER/SwapParty] swap party -- party to a swap and therefore a legal party to the contract that embodies that transaction
[DER/SwapPayingParty] swap paying party -- swap party responsible for making payments for a given leg of the transaction as defined in the contract  Also a subclass of: DER/SwapParty.
[DER/SwapReceivingParty] swap receiving party -- swap party that receives payments for a given leg of the transaction as defined in the contract  Also a subclass of: DER/SwapParty.
[DER/SwapTerms] swap terms -- legal contractual terms of a swap transaction
[DER/Swaption] swaption -- over-the-counter option that confers the right but not the obligation, to enter into a swap transaction at some time in the future
[DER/TotalReturnLeg] total return leg -- return leg based on the income generated by the underlying asset as well as any appreciation, decrease in value, capital gains, and fees on any increase in value
[DER/TotalReturnSwap] total return swap -- return swap where the seller agrees to pay the other party the difference in value of some underlying asset multiplied by an agreed-upon notional value should the asset value increase between specified periods of time  Also a subclass of: DER/ReturnSwap.
[DER/TrackerCertificate] tracker certificate -- certificate that reflects underlying price moves 1:1 (adjusted by conversion ratio and any related fees), in which the associated risk is comparable to direct investment in the underlying asset(s)
[DER/TraditionalWarrant] traditional warrant -- warrant that gives the holder the right, but not the obligation, to buy (call warrant) or to sell (put warrant) an underlying asset at a specified price (the strike or exercise price) by a predetermined date, issued by the issuer of the underlying instrument
[DER/TriggeringEvent] triggering event -- event that relates to or triggers some aspect of a credit default swap
[DER/TurboCertificate] turbo certificate -- certificate that acts as a leveraged security, whose price tracks an underlying financial asset's price one for one, and that can be used to go long or short
[DER/TwinWinCertificate] twin-win certificate -- certificate that makes profits possible with rising and falling underlying asset values, in which a falling underlying asset price converts into profit up to the barrier, and whose minimum redemption is equal to the nominal value provided the barrier has not been breached
[DER/UnderlyingAssetValuation] underlying asset valuation -- assessment activity to estimate the value of an underlying asset of a derivative
[DER/UniqueProductIdentifier] unique product identifier -- sequence of characters uniquely identifying an OTC derivative product that is reportable to a trade repository
[DER/UniqueProductIdentifierRegistryEntry] unique product identifier registry entry -- entry in a unique product identifier registry
[DER/UniqueProductIdentifierServiceProvider] unique product identifier service provider -- organization designated by an external body of financial regulators to assign UPIs and operate a UPI reference data library
[DER/UniqueSwapIdentifier] unique swap identifier -- identifier for a swap that is used in recordkeeping and swap data reporting
[DER/ValuationTerms] valuation terms -- contract terms specific to valuation of the underlying asset(s)
[DER/VanillaOption] vanilla option -- common option giving the buyer (holder) the right, but not the obligation, to buy (via a call option) or sell (via a put option) the underlying assets specified at a pre-determined price (i.e., the strike price, fixed or calculated), on or before a specified date (the expiration date)
[DER/Warrant] warrant -- entitlement that permits the holder to purchase a specified amount of a financial instrument, commodity, currency or other asset during a specified period at a specified price
[DER/WeatherDerivative] weather derivative -- derivative instrument whose primary underlying notional item is based on something related to the weather, for example, the average temperature in Chicago in January  Also a subclass of: FBC/DerivativeInstrument.
[DER/YieldEnhancementProduct] yield-enhancement product -- structured product that provides a predefined yield in return for a downside risk
[DER/ZeroCouponInterestRateSwap] zero coupon interest rate swap -- interest rate swap in which the fixed rate cash flows are compounded and paid once on the expiration date, rather than periodically; the payments on the other side (which can be based on a floating interest rate or a fixed rate) follow typical swap payment schedules
[FBC/ABAIINRegistryEntry] ABA IIN registry entry -- an entry in the ABA IIN registry, a repository of financial institution characteristics collected by the ABA for those institutions to which they issue IINs
[FBC/ABARTNRegistryEntry] ABA RTN registry entry -- an entry in the ABA RTN registry, a repository of financial institution characteristics collected by the ABA Registrar on behalf of the ABA
[FBC/Account] account -- container for records associated with a business arrangement for regular transactions and services
[FBC/AccountAsAnAsset] account as an asset -- financial asset in the form of an account
[FBC/AccountHolder] account holder -- party that owns an account
[FBC/AccountIdentifier] account identifier -- identifier that denotes an account
[FBC/AccountingTransaction] accounting transaction -- event recognized by an entry in the records of an account
[FBC/AccountOwnership] account ownership -- holding of an account
[FBC/AccountProvider] account provider -- party that provides and services an account
[FBC/AccountSpecificServiceAgreement] account-specific service agreement -- service-agreement that is account-specific, applicable in cases where a client might hold multiple accounts with differing terms and conditions
[FBC/AccountStatement] account statement -- periodic summary of account activity for a given period of time
[FBC/Accrual] accrual -- the process of accumulating interest or other income that has been earned but not paid
[FBC/AccruedInterest] accrued interest -- amount of interest that has been incurred, as of a specific date, on a loan or other financial obligation but has not yet been paid out
[FBC/AdjustedClosingPrice] adjusted closing price -- amended closing price to reflect a security's value after accounting for any corporate actions, such as stock splits, dividends, and rights offerings
[FBC/AgencyAgreement] agency agreement -- agreement that designates a party as a registered agent to represent and act on behalf of another party in some, typically legal, financial, or medical capacity
[FBC/AgencyOfAForeignBankingOrganization] agency of a foreign banking organization -- place of business of a foreign bank, located in any state, at which credit balances are maintained, checks are paid, money is lent, or, to the extent not prohibited by state or federal law, deposits are accepted from a person or entity that is not a citizen or resident of the United States
[FBC/AgentForServiceOfProcess] agent for service of process -- registered agent (person or organization) designated by a business entity, such as a corporation, to receive legal correspondence on behalf of the business entity in the jurisdiction in which the agent's address is located
[FBC/AgreementCorporation] agreement corporation -- corporation chartered by a state to engage in international banking, so named because the corporation enters into an 'agreement' with the Fed's Board of Governors that it will limit its activities to those permitted
[FBC/AgreementCorporation-Banking] agreement corporation - banking -- agreement corporation whose charter allows the corporation to engage in international banking  Also a subclass of: FBC/AgreementCorporation.
[FBC/AgreementCorporation-Investment] agreement corporation - investment -- agreement corporation whose charter allows the corporation to engage in international investment banking  Also a subclass of: FBC/AgreementCorporation.
[FBC/AlternativeTradingSystem] alternative trading system -- trading venue that is more loosely regulated than a regulated exchange
[FBC/Amortization] amortization -- the process of reduction of debt or other costs through periodic charges to assets or liabilities, such as through principal payments on mortgages
[FBC/AmortizationSchedule] amortization schedule -- schedule of periodic payments (repayment installments) that specify changes in the balance of the debt over time  Also a subclass of: FND/PaymentSchedule.
[FBC/ApprovedPublicationArrangement] approved publication arrangement -- data reporting services provider that is authorized to provide the service of publishing certain trade reports on behalf of banks, investment firms, or asset management companies
[FBC/ApprovedReportingMechanism] approved reporting mechanism -- data reporting services provider that is authorized to provide the service of reporting details of transactions to competent authorities or ESMA (the European Securities and Markets Authority) on behalf of investment firms
[FBC/AuctionMarket] auction market -- exchange in which buyers and sellers submit competitive bids that do not involve direct negotiations between parties, as part of an auction scheduled either on demand or on a periodic basis
[FBC/Balance] balance -- amount of money available or owed
[FBC/Bank] bank -- depository institution, usually a corporation, that accepts deposits, makes loans, pays checks, and performs related services, for individual members of the public, businesses or other organizations
[FBC/BankAccountIdentifier] bank account identifier -- identifier that identifies a demand deposit account provided by a bank
[FBC/BankersBank] bankers' bank -- commercial bank owned exclusively (except to the extent directors' qualifying shares are required by law) by other depository institutions or depository institution holding companies, the activities of which are limited by its articles of association exclusively to providing services to or for other depository institutions, their holding companies, and the officers, directors, and employees of such institutions and companies, and to providing correspondent banking services at the request of other depository institutions or their holding companies  Also a subclass of: FBC/USBank.
[FBC/BankersBankNotSubjectToReserveRequirements] bankers' bank that is not subject to reserve requirements -- bankers' bank whose activities are not limited by specific requirements of the Federal Reserve
[FBC/BankersBankSubjectToReserveRequirements] bankers' bank subject to reserve requirements -- bankers' bank whose activities are limited by specific requirements of the Federal Reserve
[FBC/BankHoldingCompany] bank holding company -- any company that owns and/or has direct or indirect control of one or more banks; BHCs may also own nonbanking subsidiaries such as broker-dealers and asset managers  Also a subclass of: FBC/FinancialServiceProvider.
[FBC/BankIdentifier] bank identifier -- identifier that uniquely identifies the financial institution and, when appropriate, the branch of that financial institution servicing an account
[FBC/BankingProduct] banking product -- product provided to consumers and businesses by a depository institution
[FBC/BankingService] banking service -- financial service offered by a depository institution
[FBC/Bankruptcy] bankruptcy -- credit event involving a change in state or condition in which a party becomes insolvent
[FBC/BasicBankAccountIdentifier] basic bank account identifier -- identifier that uniquely identifies an individual account at a specific financial institution in a particular country and which includes a bank identifier of the financial institution servicing that account
[FBC/Basket] basket -- collection of goods, services, or other things (e.g., financial contracts) that can be purchased and sold in some marketplace
[FBC/BasketConstituent] basket constituent -- component of a basket
[FBC/BestBid] best bid -- highest bid price a prospective buyer is willing to pay at a particular time for a given security

[FBC/BidAskSpread] bid ask spread -- difference between an offer (ask) price and a bid price
[FBC/BidPrice] bid price -- price a prospective buyer is willing to pay
[FBC/Borrower] borrower -- party to a credit agreement that is obligated to repay the amount borrowed (principal) with interest and other fees according to the terms of the instrument  Also a subclass of: FND/ContractParty, FND/Customer.
[FBC/BorrowerIdentificationScheme] borrower identification scheme -- system for allocating identifiers to borrowers
[FBC/BorrowerIdentifier] borrower identifier -- sequence of characters, capable of uniquely identifying a borrower
[FBC/BorrowingCapacity] borrowing capacity -- upper bound on the total amount of money that a lender believes a party has the ability to repay an obligation when due, as of some point in time
[FBC/BranchOfADepositoryInstitution] branch of a depository institution -- any office or any place of business located in any State of the United States at which deposits are received
[FBC/Broker] broker -- any party that acts as an intermediary between a buyer and a seller, usually charging a commission
[FBC/BrokerageAccount] brokerage account -- account offered by a broker that allows the investor to deposit funds and place investment orders
[FBC/BrokerageFirm] brokerage firm -- firm in the business of buying and selling securities, operating as both a broker and a dealer, depending on the transaction  Also a subclass of: FBC/BrokerDealer.
[FBC/BrokerDealer] broker-dealer -- any party in the business of buying and selling securities, operating as both a broker and a dealer, depending on the transaction
[FBC/BusinessCenterCode] business center code -- code used to denote a metropolitan area where business is conducted
[FBC/BusinessCenterCodeScheme] business center code set -- coding scheme used to define a set of codes for municipalities or business centers
[FBC/BusinessDayAdjustmentCode] business day adjustment code -- code used to denote a convention for specifying what happens when a date falls on a day that is weekend or holiday in some municipality or business center
[FBC/BusinessIdentifierCode] business identifier code -- international identifier for financial and non-financial institutions used to facilitate automated processing of information for financial services

[FBC/BusinessIdentifierCodeScheme] business identifier code scheme -- scheme that specifies the elements of a unique business identifier code (BIC) scheme to identify financial and non-financial institutions used to facilitate automated processing of information for financial services
[FBC/BusinessNumber] business number -- unique, 9-digit number that is the standard identifier for legal entities in Canada which are typically a business
[FBC/BusinessPartyPrefix] business party prefix -- four-character (4 alphanumeric) code associated with an organization for the purposes of banking telecommunications
[FBC/BusinessPartySuffix] business party suffix -- two-character (2 alphanumeric) code associated with the organization for the purposes of banking telecommunications
[FBC/BusinessRegisterIdentifier] business register identifier -- identifier that uniquely identifies a business register, such as a register identified by the Global Legal Entity Identifier Foundation (GLEIF) registration authorities list
[FBC/BusinessRegistrationAuthority] business registration authority -- registration authority that is responsible for maintaining a registry of business entities
[FBC/BusinessRegistry] business registry -- registry for registering and maintaining information about business entities
[FBC/BusinessRegistryEntry] business registry entry -- entry in a business registry
[FBC/CalculationAgent] calculation agent -- party that is responsible for determining the value of an instrument and in some cases, determines how much the parties owe one another
[FBC/CanadianCreditUnion] Canadian credit union -- not-for-profit financial institution, typically formed by the employees of a company, labor union, or religious group, operated as a cooperative association organized for the purpose of promoting thrift among its members and creating a source of credit for provident or productive purposes
[FBC/CapitalLease] capital lease -- lease that must be reflected on an organization's balance sheet as an asset and as a corresponding liability
[FBC/CashInstrument] cash instrument -- financial instrument whose value is determined by the market and that is readily transferable (highly liquid)
[FBC/CashSettlementTerms] cash settlement terms -- contractual commitment to settle in cash
[FBC/Catalog] catalog -- publication including a list of products available for sale with their descriptions and possibly prices
[FBC/CentralBank] central bank -- financial institution that is the monetary authority and major regulatory bank for a country (or group of countries)  Also a subclass of: FBC/MonetaryAuthority.
[FBC/CentralCounterpartyClearingHouse] central counterparty clearing house -- clearing house that helps facilitate trading in derivatives and equities markets
[FBC/CentralSecuritiesDepository] central securities depository -- functional entity that provides a central point for depositing financial instruments ('securities'), for example, bonds and shares
[FBC/CertificateOfDeposit] certificate of deposit -- cash instrument associated with a time deposit account that cannot be withdrawn for a certain period of time (term)
[FBC/ChartOfAccounts] chart of accounts -- structured system of financial account codes used to classify, record, and organize an entity's financial transactions in accordance with applicable legal, regulatory, and reporting requirements
[FBC/CleanPrice] clean price -- debt instrument price that does not include accrued interest
[FBC/ClearingBank] clearing bank -- commercial bank that facilitates payment and settlement of financial transactions, such as check clearing or facilitating trades between the sellers and buyers of securities or other financial instruments or contracts  Also a subclass of: FBC/CommercialBank.
[FBC/ClearingCorporation] clearing corporation -- clearing house that is organized as a corporation
[FBC/ClearingHouse] clearing house -- financial service provider that is exchange affiliated and provides clearing services, including the validation, delivery, and settlement of financial transactions, for financial intermediaries
[FBC/ClearingService] clearing service -- service provided on behalf of an institutional market participant by a clearing services provider following a trade that finalizes the transfer of security ownership
[FBC/CloseDate] close date -- date on which something was closed
[FBC/ClosingPrice] closing price -- cash value of the last transacted price before the market closes
[FBC/ClosingPriceDeterminationMethod] closing price determination method -- strategy for calculating or otherwise determining an official closing price
[FBC/Collateral] collateral -- something pledged as security to ensure fulfillment of an obligation to another party, to lend money, extend credit, or provision securities
[FBC/CollateralizedGuaranty] collateralized guaranty -- guaranty that takes the form of some asset that is pledged by a borrower to a lender (usually in return for a loan)
[FBC/CollateralValueAsOfDate] collateral value as of date -- appraised value of the collateral for an obligation as of a given date
[FBC/CollectionOfSecurityPrices] collection of security prices -- collection consisting of a series of prices, each of which has a specific date and time associated with it, for some security
[FBC/CommercialBank] commercial bank -- depository institution that engages in various financial services, such as accepting deposits and making loans
[FBC/CommercialFinanceCompany] commercial finance company -- finance company that makes loans to manufacturers and wholesalers, secured by accounts receivable, inventories, and equipment
[FBC/CommercialLendingCompany] commercial lending company -- any institution, other than a bank or an organization operating under section 25 of the Federal Reserve Act [12 U.S.C. 601 et seq.], organized under the laws of any State of the United States, or the District of Columbia which maintains credit balances incidental to or arising out of the exercise of banking powers and engages in the business of making commercial loans
[FBC/CommercialLendingService] commercial lending service -- service involving the extension of credit to support business activities
[FBC/CommittedCreditFacility] committed credit facility -- credit facility that is a confirmed source of financing for the borrower, as long as the borrower meets the conditions of the agreement
[FBC/CommittedSubFacility] committed sub-facility -- contractually committed portion of a credit facility that is available to the borrower and may be associated with some specific collateral
[FBC/CommodityInstrument] commodity instrument -- financial instrument representing an ownership interest in bulk goods, such as raw materials and primary agricultural products
[FBC/CommodityTradingAdvisor] commodity trading advisor -- party that directly or indirectly advises others as to the value or advisability of buying or selling futures contracts or options
[FBC/CompositeMarket] composite market -- group of exchanges and trading venues referenced for pricing purposes
[FBC/ConsolidatedTapeProvider] consolidated tape provider -- data reporting services provider that is authorized to provide the service of collecting trade reports for financial instruments from regulated markets, MTFs, OTFs and APAs and consolidating them into a continuous electronic live data stream providing price and volume data per financial instrument
[FBC/ConsumerFinanceCompany] consumer finance company -- finance company that lends to individuals under the small loans laws of the jurisdiction in which they operate
[FBC/ContractLifecycle] contract lifecycle -- lifecycle of an agreement, including, but not limited to a credit agreement, financial instrument, or other formal contract, from initial stages through retirement
[FBC/ContractLifecycleEvent] contract lifecycle event -- kind of event that occurs during one or more stages of the lifecycle of an agreement
[FBC/ContractLifecycleEventOccurrence] contract lifecycle event occurrence -- actual occurrence of an event during a specific stage of a specific contract lifecycle
[FBC/ContractLifecycleOccurrence] contract lifecycle occurrence -- realization of the lifecycle of a specific contract
[FBC/ContractLifecycleStage] contract lifecycle stage -- phase in the lifecycle of an agreement
[FBC/ContractLifecycleStageOccurrence] contract lifecycle stage occurrence -- realization, from start to finish of a phase in an occurrence of a specific contract lifecycle
[FBC/ContractualSavingsInstitution] contractual savings institution -- financial institution that provides the opportunity for individuals to invest in collective investment vehicles in a fiduciary rather than a principle role  Also a subclass of: FBC/NonDepositoryInstitution.
[FBC/CooperativeBank] cooperative bank -- state-chartered savings association that is organized and operates according to the laws of the state in which it is chartered or organized, including Massachusetts, New Hampshire, Rhode Island or Vermont
[FBC/CorporationIncomeTaxNumber] corporation income tax number -- concatenation of an entity's business number, the 'RC' abbreviation and a 4-digit subaccount number used for reporting corporate income tax
[FBC/CRDCreditInstitution] CRD credit institution -- an undertaking whose business is to receive deposits or other repayable funds from the public and to grant credits for its own account as defined by the European Banking Authority (EBA)
[FBC/CreditAgreement] credit agreement -- contractual agreement in which a debtor receives something of value and typically agrees to repay the creditor by some date in the future, in some form (e.g., cash, securities, etc.), generally with interest
[FBC/CreditAgreementRepaidAtMaturity] credit agreement repaid at maturity -- credit agreement in which accrued interest may be periodically repaid or paid at maturity, but principal is paid at maturity
[FBC/CreditAgreementRepaidPeriodically] credit agreement repaid periodically -- credit agreement in which the principal and accrued interest may be periodically repaid or exchanged
[FBC/CreditEnhancementAgreement] credit enhancement agreement -- collateral agreement that governs the exchange of collateral between parties to mitigate counterparty credit risk
[FBC/CreditEnhancementBeneficiary] credit enhancement beneficiary -- party that benefits from the collateral or guarantee established under the agreement, i.e., that is protected against counterparty credit risk because the collateral or guarantee serves as security for the obligation(s) owed to them  Also a subclass of: FND/Counterparty.
[FBC/CreditEvent] credit event -- event signifying a sudden change in credit standing, such as bankruptcy or a violation of a bond indenture or loan agreement, that raises doubts about the party's ability to meet current or future obligations
[FBC/CreditFacility] credit facility -- credit agreement that allows the borrower to periodically take out money over an extended period of time rather than reapplying for a loan every time they need funds
[FBC/CreditInquiry] credit inquiry -- request from a lender to a credit repository to obtain information regarding a prospective borrower's creditworthiness
[FBC/CreditInquiryType] credit inquiry type -- classifier indicating whether a credit inquiry is a result of a borrower's direct authorization or by some indirect means
[FBC/CreditInstitution] credit institution -- an undertaking the business of which is to take deposits or other repayable funds from the public and to grant credits for its own account, and to which authorisation has been granted to operate within the European Union and European Economic Area countries (EEA)
[FBC/CreditInstitutionInvestmentFirm] credit institution / investment firm -- classification specific to European financial institutions that designates them as credit institutions / investment firms as defined by the European Banking Authority (EBA)
[FBC/CreditInstitutionRegisterEntry] Credit Institution Register entry -- entry in the Credit Institution Register, a repository of credit institutions collected by the European Banking Authority (EBA) as provided by the various national banking authorities for those institutions that qualify
[FBC/CreditMessage] credit message -- notice on a credit report to alert a reviewer of special or exceptional information
[FBC/CreditMessageType] credit message type -- classifier that categorizes credit messages
[FBC/Creditor] creditor -- a party to whom an obligation, such as an amount of money, or good, or performance of some service exists
[FBC/CreditQuality] credit quality -- classifier for borrowers, rates, or holdings in the lending market with respect to the quality of the credit
[FBC/CreditRating] credit rating -- assessment of creditworthiness of a borrower generally or with respect to a particular debt or financial obligation
[FBC/CreditRatingAgency] credit rating agency -- rating agency that publishes reports assessing the creditworthiness of a borrower or legal entity, either generally or with respect to a specific obligation  Also a subclass of: FND/RatingAgency.
[FBC/CreditRatingModel] credit rating model -- algorithm for computing a credit rating
[FBC/CreditRatingModelType] credit score model type -- a type corresonding to a family of credit scoring algorithms sharing common characteristics
[FBC/CreditRatingScale] credit rating scale -- rating scale for assigning a credit rating to individual, entity, or instrument, including defining a set of codes or numeric scores and indicating how an assessment that is assigned a score based on that scale means
[FBC/CreditReport] credit report -- report describing the creditworthiness and related credit attributes of a borrower
[FBC/CreditReportCategory] credit report category -- classifier for credit reports, often available from multiple vendors
[FBC/CreditReportProduct] credit report product -- branded credit report offered in the marketplace  Also a subclass of: FND/OffTheShelfProduct.
[FBC/CreditTradeline] credit tradeline -- report derived from the transaction history of a credit account
[FBC/CreditUnion] credit union -- not-for-profit depository institution that makes personal loans and offers other consumer banking services, organized for the purpose of promoting thrift among its members and creating a source of credit for provident or productive purposes  Also a subclass of: FBC/DepositoryInstitution.
[FBC/CreditWatchDirection] credit watch direction
[FBC/CreditWatchOutlook] credit watch outlook
[FBC/CrossDefaultProvision] cross default provision -- contract provision that triggers a default under one contract if the borrower defaults on another related obligation
[FBC/CryptoAssetServicesProvider] crypto asset services provider -- financial services provider that provides services for crypto assets that enable the control of crypto assets, and participate in, or provide, financial services for issuers' offers, or sale, of crypto assets
[FBC/CurrencyInstrument] currency instrument -- financial instrument used for the purposes of currency trading
[FBC/CustomerAccount] customer account -- account that represents an identified, named collection of balances and cumulative totals used to summarize customer transaction-related activity over a designated period of time
[FBC/CustomerAccountHolder] customer account holder -- party that owns a customer account
[FBC/DarkPool] dark pool -- privately organized alternative trading system, that allows institutional investors the ability to trade without exposure until after the trade has been executed and reported
[FBC/DataProcessingService] data processing service -- financial service offered by an entity primarily engaged in providing infrastructure for hosting or data processing services
[FBC/DataProcessingServicer] data processing servicer -- finance services provider primarily engaged in providing infrastructure for hosting or data processing services
[FBC/DataReportingServicesProvider] data reporting services provider -- market data provider and reporting party that reports and/or publishes data on securities transactions, including required regulatory reporting for such transactions, and as such is subject to regulatory supervision  Also a subclass of: FND/ReportingParty.
[FBC/DayCountConvention] day-count convention -- a business recurrence interval convention that is used to calculate the number of days in an interest payment, which applies to the amount of accrued interest or the present value for debt instruments
[FBC/Dealer] dealer -- any party that purchases goods or services for resale and acts on their own behalf in a transaction
[FBC/Debt] debt -- obligation to pay something, such as an amount of money, good, service, or instrument
[FBC/DebtInstrument] debt instrument -- financial instrument and credit agreement evidencing monies owed by the issuer to the holder on terms as specified  Also a subclass of: FBC/FinancialInstrument.
[FBC/Debtor] debtor -- a party that owes a debt or other obligation to another party
[FBC/DebtTerms] debt terms -- contract terms that specify the formal rights and obligations of borrower and lender under a contract in which funds are lent from the one party to the other
[FBC/DefaultEvent] default event -- credit event representing a failure to meet a contractual obligation, such as failure to repay a debt including interest or principal on a loan or security
[FBC/DeliveryMethod] delivery method -- method and commitment to transfer a commodity, currency, security, cash or another instrument as defined in the settlement terms of the contract
[FBC/DemandDepositAccount] demand deposit account -- non-interest-bearing deposit account in which deposits are payable immediately on demand, or that are issued with an original maturity or required notice period of less than seven days, or that represent funds for which the depository institution does not reserve the right to require at least seven days' written notice of an intended withdrawal
[FBC/DepositAccount] deposit account -- account that provides a record of money placed with a depository institution for safekeeping and management  Also a subclass of: FBC/InvestmentOrDepositAccount.
[FBC/DepositoryInstitution] depository institution -- any financial institution engaged in the business of receiving demand deposits from the public or other institutions
[FBC/DerivativeInstrument] derivative instrument -- financial instrument that confers on its holders certain rights or obligations, whose value is derived from one or more underlying assets
[FBC/DerivedPrice] derived price -- price that stems from another source or calculation rather than being quoted or based on actual trading data  Also a subclass of: FND/CalculatedPrice.
[FBC/DesignatedContractMarket] designated contract market -- exchange, trading system, or platform that enables listing for trading futures or option contracts based on any underlying commodity, index or instrument
[FBC/DevelopmentBank] development bank -- national or regional financial institution designed to provide medium- and long-term capital for productive investment, often accompanied by technical assistance, in poor countries
[FBC/DirtyPrice] dirty price -- debt instrument price that includes accrued interest
[FBC/DistressedRatingsDowngrade] distressed ratings downgrade -- credit event triggered when the credit rating of an obligation is downgraded to a distressed debt level
[FBC/DomesticBranchOfAForeignBank] domestic branch of a foreign bank -- place of business of a foreign bank, located in any state, at which deposits are received, and that is not an agency as defined in https://www.ecfr.gov/current/title-12/chapter-II/subchapter-A/part-211/subpart-B/section-211.21  Also a subclass of: FBC/OfficeOfAForeignBank.
[FBC/DomesticBranchOfDomesticBank] domestic branch of domestic bank -- branch that resides in the United States, and whose parent is also located in the United States
[FBC/DomesticEntity] domestic entity -- financial service provider that is incorporated and domiciled in the United States
[FBC/DomesticEntityOther] domestic entity other -- domestic institution that engages in banking activities usually in connection with the business of banking in the United States
[FBC/DomesticNonBankSubsidiaryOfADomesticEntity] domestic non-bank subsidiary of a domestic entity -- non-bank financial service provider based in the United States of which 25 percent or more of whose voting shares are owned or controlled by an entity that is also based in the United States, or of which a majority of its directors are controlled by such domestic entity, or of which 25 percent or more of whose voting shares are held by trustees for the benefit of the shareholders or members of such domestic entity  Also a subclass of: FBC/NonBankSubsidiaryOfADomesticEntity.
[FBC/Downgrade] downgrade -- credit event triggered when the credit rating of a party or obligation is lowered
[FBC/EdgeCorporation] edge corporation -- corporation chartered by the Federal Reserve to engage in international banking and financial operations
[FBC/EdgeCorporation-Banking] edge corporation - banking -- edge corporation whose charter allows the corporation to engage in international banking  Also a subclass of: FBC/EdgeCorporation.
[FBC/EdgeCorporation-DomesticBranch] edge corporation - domestic branch -- branch of an edge corporation that is located in the United States
[FBC/EdgeCorporation-Investment] edge corporation - investment -- edge corporation whose charter allows the corporation to engage in international investment banking  Also a subclass of: FBC/EdgeCorporation.
[FBC/ElectronicCommunicationNetwork] electronic communication network -- alternative trading system that automatically matches buy and sell orders for securities in the market
[FBC/ElectronicFundsTransferService] electronic funds transfer service -- service involving any transfer of funds other than a transaction involving a paper instrument, that is initiated through an electronic terminal, telephone, or computer and that orders or authorizes a financial institution to debit or credit an account
[FBC/EmployerIdentificationNumber] employer identification number -- unique nine-digit number assigned by the Internal Revenue Service (IRS) to business entities operating in the United States for the purposes of identification
[FBC/EmployerIdentificationNumberingScheme] employer identification numbering scheme -- taxpayer identification numbering scheme used in the United States to identify business entities
[FBC/Entitlement] entitlement -- financial instrument that provides the holder an interest in, or the privilege to subscribe to, or to receive specific assets under terms specified
[FBC/EntityExpirationReason] entity expiration reason -- code for the reason that a legal entity ceased to exist and/or operate
[FBC/EntityLegalFormRegistry] entity legal form registry -- registry for registering and maintaining information about the legal forms that are valid for business entities for a particular jurisdiction following the ISO 20275 standard
[FBC/EntityLegalFormRegistryEntry] entity legal form registry entry -- entry in an entity legal form registry that conforms to ISO 20275
[FBC/EntitySpecificCreditEvent] entity-specific credit event -- credit event that applies to a given legal person
[FBC/EntityStatus] entity status -- lifecycle stage indicating the operational and/or legal status of an entity
[FBC/EntityValidationLevel] entity validation level -- code for the level of validation performed by the GLEIF or LOU with respect to the reference data provided by the registrant
[FBC/EquityInstrument] equity instrument -- financial instrument representing an ownership interest in an entity or pool of assets
[FBC/EuropeanEconomicAreaBranch] European Economic Area branch -- a branch of a credit institution authorised in another European Economic Area (EEA) country that has the right to passport its activities
[FBC/Examiner] examiner -- party empowered as an official representative by a regulatory agency to investigate and review specified documents for accuracy and truthfulness
[FBC/Exchange] exchange -- any organization, association, or group of persons, whether incorporated or unincorporated, which constitutes, maintains, or provides a facility for bringing together purchasers and sellers of financial instruments, commodities, or other products, services, or goods, and includes the market place and facilities maintained by such exchange
[FBC/ExchangeParticipant] exchange participant -- registered agent who, in accordance with the rules of an exchange, may trade on or through the exchange and whose name is entered in a list, register or roll kept by the exchange as an agent who may trade on or through the exchange
[FBC/ExemptSecurity] exempt security -- security that is exempt from certain regulatory rules
[FBC/ExplicitContractEventSchedule] explicit contract event schedule -- schedule of events, including but not limited to payment events, rate reset events and others that will occur over the lifetime of the credit agreement
[FBC/Exposure] exposure -- the extent to which an individual or organization is unprotected and open to damage, danger, risk of suffering a loss, or uncertainty
[FBC/FaceAmountCertificateCompany] face amount certificate company -- investment company which is engaged or proposes to engage in the business of issuing face-amount certificates of the installment type, or which has been engaged in such business and has any such certificate outstanding
[FBC/FailureToPay] failure to pay -- default event that is triggered following any applicable grace period in which a payment obligation is missed
[FBC/FailureToPayInterest] failure to pay interest -- default event that where either an expected interest payment is missed altogether or the amount paid is less than the required amount
[FBC/FailureToPayPrincipal] failure to pay principal -- default event that where either an expected principal payment is missed altogether or the amount paid is less than the required amount
[FBC/FarmCreditSystemInstitution] farm credit system institution -- federally-chartered financial institution that is supervised, examined, and regulated by the Farm Credit Administration and operates in accordance with the Farm Credit Act of 1971, as amended, 12 U.S.C. 2001 et seq  Also a subclass of: FBC/DomesticEntity.
[FBC/FDICCertificateNumber] FDIC Certificate Number -- identifier issued to a depository institution by the FDIC on approval of that institution's application for insurance
[FBC/FDICRegistryEntry] FDIC registry entry -- an entry in the FDIC institution directory, a repository of financial institution characteristics collected by the FDIC related to the institutions they insure
[FBC/FederalAgencyOfForeignBankingOrganization] federal agency of foreign banking organization -- agency of a foreign bank established and operating under section 3102 of CFR Title 12, Chapter 32 and section 4 of the International Banking Act of 1978
[FBC/FederalBranchOfForeignBankingOrganization] federal branch of foreign banking organization -- branch of a foreign bank established and operating under section 3102 of CFR Title 12, Chapter 32 and section 4 of the International Banking Act of 1978
[FBC/FederalCreditUnion] federal credit union -- credit union that has a federal affiliation
[FBC/FederalGovernmentEntity] federal government entity -- formal organization that is an independent agency, instrumentality or other permanent or semi-permanent organization in the machinery of government in the United States, authorized by the executive branch or by Congress, that operates at the national (federal) level
[FBC/FederalReserveDistrict] Federal Reserve district -- a region of the US identifying the jurisdiction of a Federal Reserve Bank, numbered and named for the city in which that reserve bank is located
[FBC/FederalReserveDistrictBank] Federal Reserve district bank -- Federal Reserve district and member bank, with jurisdiction over a specific region of the US, named for the city in which the reserve bank is located  Also a subclass of: FBC/FederalReserveSystemMember.
[FBC/FederalReserveDistrictIdentifier] Federal Reserve district identifier -- identifier associated with a Federal Reserve district
[FBC/FederalReserveSystemMember] Federal Reserve System member -- financial institution that is a member of the Federal Reserve System (FRS)
[FBC/FederalReserveSystemNonMemberInstitution] Federal Reserve System non-member institution -- depository institution that is not member of the Federal Reserve System (FRS)
[FBC/FederalSavingsBank] federal savings bank -- savings bank that has a federal affiliation
[FBC/Fee] fee -- charge for services performed
[FBC/FilingForBankruptcy] filing for bankruptcy -- credit event that involves a request to a court to be recognized as bankrupt
[FBC/FinanceCompany] finance company -- financial intermediary in the business of making loans that obtains its financing from banks, institutions, and other money market sources rather than from deposits
[FBC/FinancialExposure] financial exposure -- the extent to which an individual or organization is open to risk of suffering a loss in a transaction, or with respect to some investment or set of investments, e.g., some holding; the amount one stands to lose in that transaction or investment
[FBC/FinancialHoldingCompany] financial holding company -- financial entity engaged in a broad range of banking-related activities as permitted under the Gramm-Leach-Bliley Act of 1999
[FBC/FinancialInstitution] financial institution -- financial service provider identified as either a government agency or privately owned entity that collects funds from the public and from other institutions, and invests those funds in financial assets, such as loans, securities, bank deposits, and income-generating property
[FBC/FinancialInstrument] financial instrument -- written contract that gives rise to both a financial asset of one entity and a financial liability of another entity
[FBC/FinancialInstrumentIdentifier] financial instrument identifier -- sequence of characters uniquely identifying a financial instrument for some purpose and within a specified context
[FBC/FinancialIntermediationService] financial intermediation service -- any financial service in which a third party (the intermediary) matches lenders and investors with entrepreneurs and other borrowers in need of capital
[FBC/FinancialProduct] financial product -- product provided to consumers and businesses by financial institutions such as banks, insurance companies, brokerage firms, consumer finance companies, and investment companies
[FBC/FinancialProductCatalog] financial product catalog -- catalog of financial products and/or services available for sale with their description and other product details
[FBC/FinancialService] financial service -- service provided to consumers and businesses by financial institutions such as banks, insurance companies, brokerage firms, consumer finance companies, and investment companies
[FBC/FinancialServiceProvider] financial service provider -- functional entity either licensed to provide financial services to consumers and/or businesses or established by law to provide financial services, such as a central bank
[FBC/FinancialServiceProviderIdentifier] financial service provider identifier -- identifier that is officially allocated to a financial service provider based on a function that they provide, typically in a jurisdiction over which a regulatory agency has some jurisdiction
[FBC/FinancialServiceProviderIdentifierScheme] financial service provider identifier scheme -- scheme that defines the financial service provider identifier per the issuing registration authority or regulatory agency
[FBC/FixedInterestRate] fixed interest rate -- interest rate that does not fluctuate over the lifetime of a loan or other debt instrument
[FBC/FloatingInterestRate] floating interest rate -- variable interest rate that is based on a specific index or benchmark rate
[FBC/ForeignBank] foreign bank -- financial institution organized under the laws of a foreign country, a territory of the United States, Puerto Rico, Guam, American Samoa, or the Virgin Islands, which engages in the business of banking, or any subsidiary or affiliate, organized under such laws, of any such institution
[FBC/ForeignBankingOrganization] foreign banking organization -- financial service provider that is headquartered outside the United States and that can acquire or establish freestanding banks or bank holding companies in the United States
[FBC/ForeignBankingOrganizationAsABankHoldingCompany] foreign banking organization as a bank holding company -- foreign banking organization that is a bank holding company in the United States  Also a subclass of: FBC/ForeignBankingOrganization.
[FBC/ForeignBankingOrganizationOfABankHoldingCompany] foreign banking organization of a bank holding company -- foreign banking organization that is owned or controlled by a bank holding company
[FBC/ForeignBranchOfForeignBank] foreign branch of foreign bank -- branch that resides outside of the United States whose parent is located outside of the United States
[FBC/ForeignBranchOfForeignBankManagedByUSOffice] foreign branch of foreign bank managed by US office -- branch that resides outside of the United States whose parent is located outside of the United States that is managed by a US branch or agency of the foreign bank
[FBC/ForeignBranchOfUSBank] foreign branch of US bank -- branch that resides outside of the United States, but has a parent that is located in the United States
[FBC/ForeignEntityOther] foreign entity other -- foreign institution that engages in banking activities usually in connection with the business of banking in the countries where such foreign institutions are organized or operating
[FBC/FullAmortization] full amortization -- amortization in which the very last payment (which, if the schedule was calculated correctly, should be equal to all others) pays off all remaining principal and interest on the loan
[FBC/Future] future -- derivative instrument that obligates the buyer to receive and the seller to deliver the assets specified at an agreed price, at some later point in time
[FBC/FuturesCommissionMerchant] futures commission merchant -- party that does both of the following: (1) solicits or accepts orders to buy or sell futures contracts, options on futures, retail off-exchange forex contracts, or swaps and (2) accepts money or other assets from customers to support such orders
[FBC/GeneralLedger] general ledger -- organized collection of ledger accounts used to record and summarize changes in position as transactions are posted during an accounting period
[FBC/GoodsServicesTaxHarmonizedSalesTaxRegistrationNumber] Goods and Services Tax / Harmonized Sales Tax registration number -- concatenation of an entity's business number, the 'RT' abbreviation and a 4-digit subaccount number used for reporting GST/HST  Also a subclass of: FBC/BusinessNumber.
[FBC/GovernmentGuaranty] government guaranty -- guaranty provided by a government entity, such as for a government-backed security
[FBC/GovernmentIssuedLicense] government-issued license -- grant of permission needed to legally perform some task, provide some service, exercise a certain privilege, or pursue some business or occupation
[FBC/Guarantor] guarantor -- party that guarantees, endorses, or provides indemnity for some obligation on behalf of some other party  Also a subclass of: FND/ContractThirdParty.
[FBC/Guaranty] guaranty -- commitment whereby something is formally assured if a party with primary liability fails to perform
[FBC/HardCreditEvent] hard credit event -- default event that is not repairable
[FBC/HighPrice] high price -- highest price for a given security over the period specified
[FBC/Holding] holding -- real or personal property (assets), including but not limited to financial assets, to which one holds title and of which one has possession
[FBC/HoldingCompany] holding company -- business entity established to own stock in another company, typically to own enough voting shares to have some level of control over that company's policies and management
[FBC/ImportExportProgramNumber] import export program number -- concatenation of an entity's business number, the 'RM' abbreviation and a 4-digit subaccount number used for customs and import/export reporting purposes
[FBC/IndividualTransaction] individual transaction -- event that has a monetary impact and is documented in the records associated with an account  Also a subclass of: FND/Occurrence.
[FBC/IndustrialBank] industrial bank -- limited service financial institution that raises funds by selling certificates called 'investment shares' and by accepting deposits
[FBC/InformationReturnsProgramNumber] information return program number -- concatenation of an entity's business number, the 'RZ' abbreviation and a 4-digit subaccount number used for information returns
[FBC/InstallmentDefault] installment default -- default event involving non-payment of several installment payments as scheduled in the terms of the agreement, or non-payment of a call by the beneficial owner
[FBC/InstrumentCreditRating] instrument credit rating -- investment credit rating that provides an opinion of creditworthiness of an instrument, typically with some relationship to the creditworthiness of the issuer(s)
[FBC/InsuranceBackedGuaranty] insurance-backed guaranty -- guaranty that is realized as an insurance policy
[FBC/InsuranceCompany] insurance company -- non-depository institution whose primary and predominant business activity is the writing of insurance or the reinsuring of risks underwritten by insurance companies, and that provides compensation based on the happening of at least one contingency
[FBC/InsurancePolicy] insurance policy -- contract that (1) puts an indemnity cover into effect, (2) serves as a legal evidence of the insurance agreement, (3) sets out the exact terms on which the indemnity cover has been provided, and (4) states associated information such as the (a) specific risks and perils covered, (b) duration of coverage, (c) amount of premium, (d) mode of premium payment, and (e) deductibles, if any
[FBC/InsuranceService] insurance service -- financial service in which the insurer promises to provide compensation for specific potential future losses in exchange for a periodic payment
[FBC/InsuredFederalBranchOfForeignBankingOrganization] insured federal branch of foreign banking organization -- any office or any place of business of a foreign bank located in any State of the United States at which deposits are received established and operating under section 4 of the International Banking Act of 1978 that is insured and regulated by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation (FDIC)
[FBC/InsuredStateBranchOfForeignBankingOrganization] insured state branch of foreign banking organization -- any office or any place of business of a foreign bank located in any State of the United States at which deposits are received, established and operating under the laws of that State that is insured and regulated by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation (FDIC)
[FBC/Insurer] insurer -- financial service provider that issues an insurance policy  Also a subclass of: FND/ContractPrincipal.
[FBC/InterdealerQuotationSystem] interdealer quotation system -- automated system for organizing and disseminating price quotes by brokers and dealer firms that facilitates electronic trading in securities
[FBC/Interest] interest -- the cost of using credit, or another's money, expressed as a rate per period of time, payable by a debtor to a creditor in consideration of the credit extended to the debtor
[FBC/InterestCalculation] interest calculation -- event reflecting the calculation of interest  Also a subclass of: FND/Calculation.
[FBC/InterestCalculationSchedule] interest calculation schedule -- regular, contract-specific schedule including the dates on which interest is calculated
[FBC/InterestObligationInLightOfDefault] interest obligation in light of default -- obligation in respect of default(s) in the performance of any payment obligation  Also a subclass of: FND/ContractualObligation.
[FBC/InterestPayment] interest payment -- event reflecting the actual payment of interest
[FBC/InterestPaymentSchedule] interest payment schedule -- regular, contract-specific schedule including the dates on which interest is due to be paid  Also a subclass of: FND/PaymentSchedule.
[FBC/InterestPaymentTerms] interest payment terms -- contract terms for payment of interest on a debt
[FBC/InterestRateReset] interest rate reset -- event reflecting a potential adjustment to an interest rate, typically corresponding to a change in the underlying benchmark interest rate or index specified in the contract
[FBC/InterestRateResetSchedule] interest rate reset schedule -- regular, contract-specific schedule including the dates on which a rate reset, and corresponding actual rate, is recalculated
[FBC/InterestRateSettingEvent] interest rate setting event -- event on which an initial rate for a given contract is set, which may be relative the the occurrence of some other contract lifecycle event, such as the execution date
[FBC/IntermediateHoldingCompany] intermediate holding company -- bank holding company established or designated by a foreign banking organization under subpart O of the Federal Reserve Board's Regulation YY (12 CFR part 252)
[FBC/InternalRateOfReturn] internal rate of return -- discount rate that results in a net present value (NPV) of zero for a series of future cash flows
[FBC/InternationalBankAccountIdentifier] international bank account identifier -- identifier for a bank account that is an expanded version of the basic bank account number (BBAN), intended for use internationally
[FBC/InternationalBankOfUSDepositoryEdgeTrustCompany] international bank of US depositary, edge, trust company -- bank that is owned or controlled by a US depository institution, Edge Act corporation or trust company
[FBC/InternationalNonBankSubsidiaryOfADomesticEntity] international non-bank subsidiary of a domestic entity -- non-bank financial service provider based outside of the United States of which 25 percent or more of whose voting shares are owned or controlled by an entity that is based in the United States, or of which a majority of its directors are controlled by such domestic entity, or of which 25 percent or more of whose voting shares are held by trustees for the benefit of the shareholders or members of such domestic entity
[FBC/IntraDayPrice] intra day price -- price for a given security at some point between the opening and official closing price on an exchange
[FBC/InvestmentAccount] investment account -- account that provides a record of deposits of funds and/or securities held at a financial institution
[FBC/InvestmentBank] investment bank -- financial service provider that acts as an underwriter or agent that serves as intermediary between the issuer of securities and the investing public
[FBC/InvestmentCompany] investment company -- any issuer which: (a) is or holds itself out as being engaged primarily, or proposes to engage primarily, in the business of investing, reinvesting, or trading in securities; (b) is engaged or proposes to engage in the business of issuing face-amount certificates of the installment type, or has been engaged in such business and has any such certificate outstanding; or (c) is engaged or proposes to engage in the business of investing, reinvesting, owning, holding, or trading in securities, and owns or proposes to acquire investment securities having a value exceeding 40 per centum of the value of such issuer&apos;s total assets (exclusive of Government securities and cash items) on an unconsolidated basis
[FBC/InvestmentCreditRating] investment credit rating -- credit rating that provides an opinion of creditworthiness of an investment, including but not limited to an instrument or organization
[FBC/InvestmentFirm] investment firm -- any legal person whose regular occupation or business is the provision of one or more investment services to third parties and/or the performance of one or more investment activities on a professional basis
[FBC/InvestmentOrDepositAccount] investment or deposit account -- account associated with a product or service that requires the account holder to provide funds for management by the account provider
[FBC/InvestmentService] investment service -- financial service designed to assist investors in using capital to create more money, either through income-producing vehicles or through more risk-oriented ventures to result in capital gains, including but not limited to providing investment advice, asset and portfolio management, and brokerage services
[FBC/Issuer] issuer -- role of a party that issues (or proposes to issue in a formal filing) one or more financial instruments
[FBC/IssuerIdentificationNumber] issuer identification number -- a numbering system that allows a credit, debit, or other card to be identified as having been issued by a particular financial institution
[FBC/JointGuaranty] joint guaranty -- guaranty provided by at least two parties, jointly and severally
[FBC/Lease] lease -- credit agreement permitting the use of real estate, equipment or another asset, such as a vehicle, by the owner of that asset (the lessor) to a user (the lessee) for a specific period of time in return for payment as specified in the agreement
[FBC/LedgerAccount] ledger account -- individual record for one element or sub-element in a ledger that records and summarizes increases, decreases, and balances associated with that specific element
[FBC/LedgerAccountClassifier] ledger account classifier -- classifier used to organize an entity's financial accounts in accordance with applicable legal, regulatory, and reporting requirements
[FBC/LegalAgent] legal agent -- any party that has been legally empowered to act on behalf of another party
[FBC/LegalEntityIdentifierRegistry] legal entity identifier registry -- registry for registering and maintaining information about business entities for a particular jurisdiction
[FBC/LegalEntityIdentifierRegistryEntry] legal entity identifier registry entry -- entry in a legal entity identifier registry that conforms to ISO 17442 and the Global Legal Entity Identifier Foundation (GLEIF) Common Data Format (CDF)
[FBC/Lender] lender -- a party that extends credit or money to a borrower with the expectation of being repaid, usually with interest  Also a subclass of: FND/ContractParty.
[FBC/LendingOfficer] lending officer -- corporate officer that has overarching responsibility for the relationship with a specific borrower or account  Also a subclass of: FBC/RelationshipManager.
[FBC/LetterOfCredit] letter of credit -- letter from a bank or other creditworthy institution guaranteeing that a buyer's payment to a seller will be received on time and for the correct amount
[FBC/LetterOfCreditGuaranty] letter of credit guaranty -- guaranty that takes the form of a letter of credit, i.e., a document issued by a bank guaranteeing the payment up to a stated amount for a specified period
[FBC/LicensedAgent] licensed agent -- any individual who is licensed to perform a legally binding function, and who has been legally empowered to act on behalf of another party  Also a subclass of: FND/Licensee.
[FBC/LimitedBranchOfAForeignBank] limited branch of a foreign bank -- branch of a foreign bank that receives only such deposits as would be permitted for a corporation organized under section 25A of the Federal Reserve Act (12 U.S.C. 611-631)
[FBC/LoanOrCreditAccount] loan or credit account -- account associated with a service in which the account holder receives funds from the account provider under certain terms and conditions for repayment
[FBC/LocalFirm] local firm -- a firm dealing for its own account on markets in financial futures or options or other derivatives and on cash markets for the sole purpose of hedging positions on derivatives markets, or dealing for the accounts of other members of those markets and being guaranteed by clearing members of the same markets, where responsibility for ensuring the performance of contracts entered into by such a firm is assumed by clearing members of the same markets  Also a subclass of: FBC/BrokerageFirm.
[FBC/LocalOperatingUnit] local operating unit -- registrar that is authorized by the Global LEI Foundation to issue legal entity identifiers
[FBC/LowPrice] low price -- lowest value for a given security over the period specified
[FBC/ManagedInterestRate] managed interest rate -- variable interest rate charged by a financial institution for borrowing that is not prescribed as a margin over base rate but is set from time to time by the institution
[FBC/ManagementCompany] management company -- investment company that sells and manages a portfolio of securities other than a face-amount certificate company or unit investment fund
[FBC/MarketCategoryClassifier] market category classifier -- classifier representing the controlled vocabulary that delineates the nature of the exchange or data reporting services provider where possible
[FBC/MarketIdentifier] market identifier -- identifier that specifies a universal method of identifying exchanges, trading platforms, regulated or non-regulated markets, and data reporting services providers as sources of prices and related information in order to facilitate automated processing
[FBC/MarketIdentifierCodeRegistryEntry] market identifier code registry entry -- entry in a market identifier code registry that conforms to ISO 10383
[FBC/MarketIdentifierCodeStatus] market indicator code status -- lifecycle stage indicating the status of the MIC code, as specified by the registration authority
[FBC/MarketLevelClassifier] market level classifier -- classifier that indicates whether the exchange or data reporting services provider is an operating level or market segment level facility
[FBC/MarketPrice] market price -- last reported price at which a security was sold
[FBC/MarketSegmentLevelMarket] market segment-level market -- section of an exchange/market/trade reporting facility that specialises in one or more specific instruments or that is regulated differently
[FBC/MarketSegmentLevelMarketIdentifier] market segment-level market identifier -- market identifier that identifies a section of an exchange/market/trade reporting facility that specialises in one or more specific instruments or that is regulated differently
[FBC/MaturityExtension] maturity extension -- credit event involving extension of payments beyond the original maturity date of the obligation
[FBC/MerchantService] merchant service -- financial service provided by a financial institution to a merchant or other business, including but not limited to managing financial transactions via a secure channel
[FBC/MidPrice] mid price -- arithmetic mean between bid and offer prices  Also a subclass of: FND/ArithmeticMean.
[FBC/MonetaryAuthority] monetary authority -- regulatory agency that controls the monetary policy, regulation and supply of money in some country or group of countries
[FBC/MoneyServicesBusiness] money services business -- any person doing business, whether or not on a regular basis or as an organized business concern, in one of the following capacities: (1) currency dealer or exchanger, (2) check casher, (3) issuer of traveler's checks, money orders, or stored value, (4) seller or redeemer of traveler's checks, money orders, or stored value, (5) money transmitter, or (6) postal service
[FBC/Moratorium] moratorium -- entity-specific credit event involving a temporary suspension of payments until related issues are resolved
