[SEC/PrivateCreditFund] private credit fund -- investment vehicle that provides loans or other forms of credit to companies, typically outside of the traditional banking system
[SEC/PrivateEquityFund] private equity fund -- investment fund used for making investments in various equity (and to a lesser extent debt) securities according to an investment strategy associated with private equity
[SEC/PrivateEquityHolding] private equity holding -- A holding of private equity.
[SEC/PrivateFund] private fund -- managed investment that cannot offer securities to the public
[SEC/PrivateLabelMBSDeal] private label m b s deal
[SEC/PrivatelyHeldShare] privately held share -- share in a security that signifies ownership in an entity that is not publicly traded
[SEC/PrivatelyPlacedDepositaryReceipt] privately placed depositary receipt -- depositary receipt that represents shares in a private placement under the SEC Rule 144-A
[SEC/PrivateOffering] private offering -- offering of securities made privately to a limited number of qualified potential investors
[SEC/PrivatePlacementMemorandum] private placement memorandum -- legal document stating the objectives, risks and terms of investment involved with a private placement
[SEC/ProprietarySecurityIdentificationScheme] proprietary security identification scheme -- security identification scheme published by a commercial entity
[SEC/ProprietarySecurityIdentifier] proprietary security identifier -- identifier supplied by a commercial entity
[SEC/Prospectus] prospectus -- formal, written offering document to sell securities that provides the facts an investor needs to make an informed investment decision
[SEC/PubliclyIssuedDebt] publicly issued debt -- an issued debt in the form of a tradable debt instrument (security)
[SEC/PublicOffering] public offering -- offering of securities for sale to the investment public, after compliance with registration requirements of the relevant regulatory authorities
[SEC/PutEvent] put event -- an event associated with the put schedule for a debt instrument, i.e., an event involving the 'put', or surrender of the instrument by the holder
[SEC/PutFeature] put feature -- redemption provision giving the holder the right, but not the obligation, to sell a specified amount of the debt instrument (i.e., redeem it), prior to maturity  Also a subclass of: FBC/RedemptionProvision.
[SEC/PutNotificationProvision] put notification provision -- a provision of a put feature defining notification requirements
[SEC/PutPremium] put premium -- an amount over par that a debt instrument holder must pay to sell the security early
[SEC/PutSchedule] put schedule -- a schedule that defines the events associated with the put feature of a debt instrument, i.e, the dates on which the debt instrument may be sold at what price by the holder
[SEC/PutWindow] put window -- an explicit period of time prior to a put date during which holder or agent must give notice to an issuer
[SEC/QualifiedDividend] qualified dividend -- dividend that falls under capital gains tax rates that are lower than the income tax rates on unqualified (ordinary) dividends
[SEC/QualifiedInvestorRestriction] qualified investor restriction -- legal holding restriction that defines the concept of a qualified investor for a given purpose and specifies that only such qualified investors may hold the security
[SEC/RateBasisConvention] rate basis convention -- basis for a percentage quoted rate as used in specifying bond call percentage amounts
[SEC/RealEstateHolding] real estate holding -- tangible asset consisting of real estate that is owned or controlled by an individual, organization, or entity for investment, operational, or strategic purposes
[SEC/RealEstateInvestmentTrust] real estate investment trust -- investment fund that offers shares/units to the public and invests in real estate directly
[SEC/RealEstateMortgageInvestmentConduit] real estate mortgage investment conduit -- special purpose vehicle that pools mortgage loans together and issues mortgage-backed securities
[SEC/RedeemablePreferredShare] redeemable preferred share -- preferred share that gives the issuer the right to redeem the stock under specified conditions
[SEC/RedeemablePreferredShareWithExtendableMaturityDate] redeemable preferred share with extendable maturity date -- redeemable preferred share with a fixed maturity date whose issuer has the option to extend the maturity date  Also a subclass of: SEC/RedeemablePreferredShare.
[SEC/RedeemablePreferredShareWithExtendableRedemptionDate] redeemable preferred share with extendable redemption date -- redeemable preferred share whose redemption date can be modified
[SEC/RedemptionEvent] redemption event -- a prescriptive event involving the return of an investor's principal in a fixed-income security, such as a preferred stock or bond, or the sale of units in a mutual fund
[SEC/RedemptionPayment] redemption payment -- repayment event involving payment of a bond's principal amount at maturity or when it is called  Also a subclass of: SEC/RedemptionEvent.
[SEC/RedemptionSchedule] redemption schedule -- repayment schedule whereby a given percentage of a bond issue is redeemed on predefined dates
[SEC/ReferToFundOrderDesk] refer to fund order desk -- Restriction requiring an investor to refer to the fund order desk prior to redeeming a fund.
[SEC/RefinitivInstrumentCode] Refinitiv instrument code -- proprietary code for financial instruments and indices owned, managed, and distributed by the London Stock Exchange Group's LSEG Financial Solutions (branded as Refinitiv)
[SEC/RegisteredSecurity] registered security -- security that is registered with some registration authority
[SEC/RegularFloaterTranche] regular floater tranche -- A floater tranche is a tranche that is keyed to an index and a spread. The spread is added to the index.
[SEC/RegulatoryCall] regulatory call -- call triggered by some regulation-specific rule
[SEC/RelativePrice] relative price -- security price specified in comparison with either a stated or market value for a debt instrument at some point in time
[SEC/RemarketableBond] remarketable bond -- corporate bond program where the coupon rate on outstanding bonds is periodically reset through an auction process  Also a subclass of: SEC/FloatingRateNote.
[SEC/RepurchaseAgreement] repurchase agreement -- agreement between two parties whereby one party lends the other a security at a specified price with a commitment to take the security back at a later date for another specified price
[SEC/ResidentialMBS] residential m b s -- Residential Mortgage-Backed Securities, which are trust certificates (bonds) backed by a pool of residential mortgage loans.

[SEC/RestrictedShare] restricted share -- share whose ownership/transfer/sale is subject to special conditions including country-specific restrictions
[SEC/RestrictedVotingShare] restricted voting share -- share that confers less than one vote per share
[SEC/RetractablePreferredShare] retractable preferred share -- preferred share that gives the owner (shareholder) the right to redeem the stock under specified conditions

[SEC/SecuredBond] secured bond -- bond that is backed by collateral, such as a tangible asset or income stream, in addition to a general promise to pay

[SEC/SecurityIdentifier] security identifier -- any publicly available identifier that is used to identify a security
[SEC/SecurityRegistry] security registry -- registry used to manage security identifiers and related information
[SEC/SecurityRegistryEntry] security registry entry -- record for a security in a securities registry
[SEC/SecurityUnderwriter] security underwriter -- party that has purchased from an issuer with a view to, or sells for an issuer in connection with, the distribution of any security, or participates or has a direct or indirect participation in any such undertaking, or participates or has a participation in the direct or indirect underwriting of any such undertaking  Also a subclass of: FBC/ThirdPartyAgent, FND/ContractThirdParty.
[SEC/SecurityUnderwritingArrangement] security underwriting arrangement -- underwriting agreement between an organization (typically an investment bank) and a securities issuer that commits the underwriter to assuming risk involved in buying a new issue of securities and reselling it to the public
[SEC/SeniorCDOTranche] senior c d o tranche -- The most senior tranche of the CDO issue. Typically rated A to AAA. If there are defaults or the CDO's collateral otherwise underperforms, scheduled payments to senior tranches take precedence over those of mezzanine tranches.  Also a subclass of: SEC/Tranche.
[SEC/SeniorMBSTranche] senior m b s tranche -- Specific kinds of tranche are modeled for example and investigation only and have been removed from the diagrams. These will be removed from the final model.
[SEC/SettlementDateRule] settlement date rule -- convention for determining settlement dates by reference to some jurisdiction or as set by a given exchange or similar venue
[SEC/Share] share -- financial instrument that signifies a unit of equity ownership in a corporation, or a unit of ownership in a mutual fund, or interest in a general or limited partnership, or a unit of ownership in a structured product, such as a real estate investment trust
[SEC/ShareIssuer] share issuer -- issuer of securities that represent an ownership interest in something
[SEC/SharePaymentStatus] share payment status -- classifier that specifies the overall payment status for shares issued
[SEC/ShareYield] share yield -- ratio of the annualized dividend per share divided by the (current) price per share
[SEC/SICAF] s i c a f -- A French fund vehicle type. Designation and definition needed.
[SEC/SICAV] s i c a v -- Societe Collective a Capital Variable
[SEC/SingleMonthlyMortality] single monthly mortality -- estimated per-month percentage of mortgages in an MBS pool that will be paid off early
[SEC/SingleVotingShare] single voting share -- share that has the right to exactly one vote
[SEC/SinkingFundAmortizationTerms] sinking fund amortization terms -- terms for the paydown of principal in a sinking fund type of amortizing security
[SEC/SoftRetractablePreferredShare] soft retractable preferred share -- retractable preferred share whose retraction value may be paid in cash or in an equal value of common stock of the issuer, at the option of the issuer
[SEC/SovereignBond] sovereign bond -- bond issued by the government of a country  Also a subclass of: SEC/SovereignDebtInstrument.
[SEC/SovereignDebtInstrument] sovereign debt instrument -- debt security issued by the government of a country
[SEC/SovereignWealthFund] sovereign wealth fund -- state-owned investment fund that consists of pools of money derived from a country's reserves
[SEC/SpecialAssessmentBond] special assessment bond -- municipal bond used to fund a development project that is payable from the revenues of an assessment (tax) on the community that is intended to benefit from the project  Also a subclass of: SEC/SecuredBond.
[SEC/SpecialDividend] special dividend -- dividend that is paid to shareholders on a one-time basis
[SEC/SpecialistMortgageIssuer] specialist mortgage issuer -- A business organization that specialises in and exists for the issuance of mortgages to the general public.
[SEC/SpecialObligationBond] special obligation bond -- bond secured by a limited revenue source, such as receipts derived from a designated project
[SEC/SpecialTaxBond] special tax bond -- bond secured by revenues derived from designated taxes other than ad valorem taxes  Also a subclass of: SEC/SecuredBond.
[SEC/SponsoredDepositaryReceipt] sponsored depositary receipt -- depositary receipt that is issued in collaboration with the foreign company enabling them to tap into international capital markets directly
[SEC/StaticCDO] static c d o -- A CDO where collateral is fixed through the life of the CDO. The reference assets are bought and then are kept untouched for the term of the product.
[SEC/StaticCDOPortfolio] static c d o portfolio -- A portfolio where collateral of the CDO is fixed through the life of the CDO. The reference assets are bought and then are kept untouched for the term of the product.
[SEC/StaticManagementStyle] static management style
[SEC/StepEvent] step event -- event that prescribes a change in a contractual term, such as a rate or notional amount, for a given contract  Also a subclass of: SEC/PrescriptiveEvent.
[SEC/SteppedCouponTerms] stepped coupon terms -- coupon payment terms for securities with a coupon that increases (steps up) while the bond is outstanding
[SEC/StepSchedule] step schedule -- schedule specifying the date(s) and change in a contractual term(s), e.g., rate or notional amount, for a contract that has a feature where stipulated changes occur at specified intervals or on specified dates
[SEC/StepUpBond] step up bond -- bond with a coupon that increases (steps up) while the bond is outstanding  Also a subclass of: SEC/FixedIncomeSecurity.
[SEC/StockExchangeDailyOfficialListCode] Stock Exchange Daily Official List (SEDOL) code -- seven-character security identifier, issued by the London Stock Exchange, that is the National Securities Identifying Number (NSIN) for securities issued in the United Kingdom, which is also part of the ISIN for the security it identifies  Also a subclass of: SEC/NationalSecuritiesIdentifyingNumber, SEC/ProprietarySecurityIdentifier.
[SEC/Strip] strip -- a tradeable debt instrument created either through the process of removing coupons from a bond and then selling the separate parts as a zero coupon bond and an interest paying coupon bond or through taking the opposite position from some variant in the options market
[SEC/StripBond] strip bond -- bond that is part of a series of bonds formed by selling each interest payment and the principal amount of a bond as separate zero coupon bonds.  Also a subclass of: SEC/Strip.
[SEC/StructuredFinanceInstrument] structured finance instrument -- pool-backed security wherein the risk associated with the pool has been uncoupled from the risk associated with the originating institution through a special purpose vehicle  Also a subclass of: DER/StructuredProduct.
[SEC/StructuredFinanceWithoutPrincipalProtection] structured finance without principal protection -- structured finance that is a short-term note linked to an underlying asset that offers a steady stream of income
[SEC/StudentLoanAssetBackedSecurity] student loan asset-backed security -- asset-backed security based on student loan receivables
[SEC/StudentLoanPool] student loan pool -- debt pool consisting of student loans
[SEC/SubordinatedCDOEquity] subordinated c d o equity -- The subordinated (also known as equity) CDO tranche is the most junior tranche in the CDO issue. If there are defaults or the CDO's collateral otherwise underperforms, scheduled payments to senior and mezzanine tranches take precedence over those to subordinated/equity tranches.
[SEC/SubordinatedMBSTranche] subordinated m b s tranche -- Specific kinds of tranche are modeled for example and investigation only and have been removed from the diagrams. These will be removed from the final model.
[SEC/SuperFloaterTranche] super floater tranche
[SEC/SuperPOTranche] super p o tranche -- Principal Only tranche. This tranche will only pay principal. Not clear how this is distinct from generic PO.
[SEC/SuperSeniorCDOTranche] super senior c d o tranche -- A tranche at the very top of a CDO Issue.
[SEC/SupportTranche] support tranche -- A tranche which provides payment support to a PAC Tranche.
[SEC/SyndicatedLoan] syndicated loan -- credit agreement in which a group of lenders, known as a syndicate, collectively provides a large loan to a single borrower  Also a subclass of: LOAN/CommercialLoan.
[SEC/SyndicationAgent] syndication agent -- financial institution (typically a commercial or investment bank) designated to help structure, arrange, and manage the loan syndication process
[SEC/SyntheticAmortizingSecurity] synthetic amortizing security -- Security constructed to emulate an amortizing security.
[SEC/SyntheticBalanceSheetCDO] synthetic balance sheet c d o -- Also a subclass of: SEC/SyntheticCDO.
[SEC/SyntheticCDO] synthetic c d o
[SEC/SyntheticCDOPortfolio] synthetic c d o portfolio
[SEC/SyntheticCDOPortfolioConstituent] synthetic c d o portfolio constituent -- An instrument which is defined as a constituent of a synthetic pool of instruments. These are not holdings because they are not held, but in all other respects they are the constituents of the portfolio.
[SEC/SyntheticCDOTranche] synthetic c d o tranche
[SEC/SyntheticDebtInstrumentPool] synthetic debt instrument pool -- A cash flow structure which synthesizes the behavior of a portfolio of debt securities. For example a synthesized portfolio of CDO / Bonds / ABS using Total Returns Swaps and CDS. This does exist, it is just manufactured from different instruments.
[SEC/SyntheticDebtInstrumentPoolFundingAsset] synthetic debt instrument pool funding asset -- An asset which provides the funding for a synthetic debt instrument pool, as used in a synthetic CDO.
[SEC/SyntheticDebtSPV] synthetic debt s p v -- A Special Purpose Vehicle set up for the issuance of synthetics CDOs. This entity (like all SPVs) its itself registered as some kind of legal entity, distinct from the sponsoring organization. It becomes the Issuer of Synthetic CDO issues.
[SEC/SyntheticPoolAsset] synthetic pool asset
[SEC/SyntheticStructuredFinanceInstrument] synthetic structured finance instrument
[SEC/TACTranche] t a c tranche -- Targeted Amortization Class. This is related to a PAC tranche and has a payment schedule geared towards a specified prepayment speed (called the pricing speed). Agency CMO  Also a subclass of: SEC/TranchedMBSInstrument.
[SEC/TACTrancheAmortizationSchedule] t a c tranche amortization schedule
[SEC/TaxAllocationBond] tax allocation bond -- bond payable from the incremental increase in tax revenues realized from any increase in property value and other economic activity, often designed to capture the economic benefit resulting from a bond financing  Also a subclass of: SEC/SecuredBond.
[SEC/TelekursId] Telekurs Id -- identifier used to identify financial instruments owned, managed, and distributed by SIX Financial Information (formerly Telekurs AG and subsequently SIX Telekurs Ltd.)
[SEC/TickerSymbol] ticker symbol -- reassignable identifier of relatively short character string length that is unique within an exchange for a particular financial instrument or listing for that instrument
[SEC/TradableDebtInstrument] tradable debt instrument -- a debt instrument that is also a security, i.e., that can be bought and sold by the holder  Also a subclass of: FBC/Security.
[SEC/TradableFundUnit] tradable fund unit -- security representing a tradable interest in a fund  Also a subclass of: FBC/NegotiableSecurity, SEC/FundUnit.
[SEC/TradingDateRule] trading date rule -- convention for determining trading dates defined with reference to some trading date calendar published by some trading facility or exchange
[SEC/TradingRestriction] trading restriction -- restriction that limits trading in some manner, typically summarized on term sheets or in other documentation, including but not limited to restrictions on day trading
[SEC/Tranche] tranche -- segment of a pool of securities, typically debt instruments
[SEC/TranchedMBSDeal] tranched m b s deal
[SEC/TranchedMBSDealProspectus] tranched m b s deal prospectus
[SEC/TranchedMBSInstrument] tranched m b s instrument
[SEC/TrancheRatingAtIssue] tranche rating at issue -- The rating at issue of a tranche of a security. Note this is under review
[SEC/TrancheType] tranche type -- the type of tranche in a tranched MBS security
[SEC/TreasuryBill] treasury bill -- short-term zero coupon treasury obligation with a maturity ranging from one to twelve months  Also a subclass of: SEC/MoneyMarketInstrument.
[SEC/TreasuryBond] treasury bond -- long term term coupon bearing treasury obligation issued in terms of 20 years or 30 years that pays interest every six months until they mature  Also a subclass of: SEC/USTreasurySecurity.
[SEC/TreasuryInflationProtectedSecurity] treasury inflation-protected security -- variable income bond whose principal is indexed to inflation or deflation and thus changes over the life of the security  Also a subclass of: SEC/USTreasurySecurity, SEC/VariablePrincipalBond.
[SEC/TreasuryNote] treasury note -- medium term coupon bearing treasury obligation with original maturity ranging from two to ten years  Also a subclass of: SEC/USTreasurySecurity.
[SEC/TriggerEvent] trigger event -- Any event where some value passes some threashold. Or some other type of business event. This is not restricted to "trigger" in the sense of a value passing a threshold. Can also be an seen such as a CDO manager going into bankruptcy.
[SEC/TruePSObjective] true p s objective
[SEC/UKGovernmentSecurity] U.K. Government security -- debt instrument issued by HM Treasury and listed on the London Stock Exchange
[SEC/UnitIssuer] unit issuer -- The party which issues the Fund Unit.
[SEC/UnitizedFund] unitized fund -- pooled investment vehicle in which investors hold units that represent a proportional share of the fund's underlying assets, typically used in pensions or insurance-based products
[SEC/UnitTrust] unit trust -- pooled investment vehicle in which investors hold units that represent beneficial ownership in a trust-managed portfolio of assets
[SEC/UnlistedBond] unlisted bond -- bond that is traded over the counter rather than via an exchange or other listing facility
[SEC/UnrestrictedShare] unrestricted share -- share whose ownership/transfer/sale is not subject to special conditions including country-specific restrictions  Also a subclass of: SEC/Share.
[SEC/UnsecuredBond] unsecured bond -- bond that is only secured by the bond issuer's good credit standing
[SEC/UnsponsoredDepositaryReceipt] unsponsored depositary receipt -- depositary receipt that is established without the company's cooperation
[SEC/USTreasuryBillAuctionDateRule] US Treasury bill auction date rule -- rule for setting auction dates for US Treasury bills
[SEC/USTreasuryBillDate] US Treasury bill date -- auction date for US 13 week and 26 week Treasury bills
[SEC/USTreasurySecurity] U.S. Treasury security -- debt instrument issued by the United States Department of the Treasury that carries a full faith and credit guarantee
[SEC/Valoren] Valoren -- identification number assigned to financial instruments in Switzerland, Liechtenstein and Belgium, issued by SIX Financial Information, that is the National Securities Identifying Number (NSIN) for securities issued in those countries and is also part of the ISIN for the security it identifies  Also a subclass of: SEC/NationalSecuritiesIdentifyingNumber, SEC/ProprietarySecurityIdentifier.
[SEC/VariableCouponBond] variable coupon bond -- bond that has a floating interest rate
[SEC/VariableCouponTerms] variable coupon terms -- contractual terms specifying the calculation of the interest rate for a variable coupon bond
[SEC/VariableDebtPrincipal] variable debt principal -- principal that is defined in relation to some variable and so varies over time, as principal
[SEC/VariableIncomeBond] variable income bond -- bond whose income may vary over time, because either the coupon rate or principal amount changes in line with an index or schedule over the life of the security  Also a subclass of: SEC/VariableIncomeSecurity.
[SEC/VariableIncomeSecurity] variable income security -- tradeable debt instrument that provide their owners with a rate of return that is dynamic and determined by market forces
[SEC/VariableInterestCalculationFormula] variable interest calculation formula -- formula for the calculation of variable interest
[SEC/VariableInterestEntityShare] variable interest entity share -- share that certifies ownership of a contractual right to a percentage of a company's profits
[SEC/VariableInterestExpression] variable interest expression -- an expression used to determine a variable interest payment amount
[SEC/VariablePrincipalBond] variable principal bond -- bond whose principal adjusts over time with changes in an index
[SEC/VotingRight] voting right -- contractual right that specifies shareholder voting entitlements, such as to elect directors, elect outside auditors, and vote on matters of corporate policy
[SEC/WeightedAverageCoupon] weighted average coupon -- weighted-average gross interest rates of the pool of mortgages that underlie a mortgage-backed security (MBS) weighed by their balances at the time the securities were issued  Also a subclass of: SEC/DebtPoolStatisticalMeasure.
[SEC/WeightedAverageLife] weighted average life -- weighted average of the times of the principal repayments Average life is calculated using the weighted average time to the receipt of all future cash flows.  Also a subclass of: SEC/DebtPoolStatisticalMeasure.
[SEC/WeightedAverageLoanAge] weighted average loan age -- dollar-weighted average measuring the age of the individual loans in a mortgage pass-through or pooled security  Also a subclass of: SEC/DebtPoolStatisticalMeasure.
[SEC/WeightedAverageMaturity] weighted average maturity -- weighted average amount of time until the maturities on mortgages in a mortgage-backed security (MBS)  Also a subclass of: SEC/DebtPoolStatisticalMeasure.
[SEC/WeightedAverageRemainingTerm] weighted average remaining term -- weighted average time to maturity of a portfolio of asset-backed securities (ABS) or mortgage-backed (MBS) securities  Also a subclass of: SEC/DebtPoolStatisticalMeasure.
[SEC/ZeroCouponBond] zero coupon bond -- bond issued with a coupon rate of zero and that trades at a deep discount to face value  Also a subclass of: SEC/FixedIncomeSecurity.
[SEC/ZeroCouponTerms] zero coupon terms -- terms for payment of interest on a zero coupon bond  Also a subclass of: SEC/FixedCouponTerms.
